The Soviet Union's Reactionary Criminals Tried; Sixteen Defendants Sentenced to Death; Only a Slim Hope of Appealing to the Central Executive Committee for Survival; Otherwise, Execution Within Seventy-Two Hours

(Moscow) The historically famous communist revolutionary leader Zinoviev, along with Kamenev, and fourteen other counter-revolutionary party members, were previously accused of being involved in the 1934 assassination of Stalin's deputy Kirov, colluding with a faction of the German secret police, engaging in espionage and terrorism, and plotting to assassinate Stalin, among other activities. The open trial in court of this shocking major case has now concluded. Today, it was announced that Zinoviev, Kamenev, and the other fourteen defendants were all sentenced to death. It is said that all the defendants confessed their guilt. However, the court deliberated in detail for eight hours before announcing the sentence of execution by shooting. After the judge read the verdict, onlookers in the courtroom cheered loudly. At present, the only hope for the defendants to survive is to appeal to the Soviet Russian Central Executive Committee, which could prevent execution within seventy-two hours of the verdict. However, during the court trial, the defendants all confessed to the charges against them. Therefore, even with the opportunity to appeal, it is feared that it may not be effective. From the perspective of the Soviet Russian government, it may be possible to pardon some of the defendants' sentences. It is said that when the court was about to announce the verdict, Kamenev spoke, warning the Soviet Russian state to remain highly vigilant in the future and not to relax its guard, because as long as Trotsky is not apprehended, Trotsky's followers will continue to invade Russian territory and implement terrorist tactics, etc. Kamenev further entrusted his three sons with his final declaration, to be conveyed to the youth of the nation, stating that Stalin is the greatest leader of the world's workers, and the youth of the country should cherish him. He also implored the youth of Soviet Russia not to follow anti-communist discipline, lest they repeat his own mistakes, etc. It is said that one of Kamenev's three sons is an aircraft pilot in the Red Army. It is claimed that during the trial of this case, many shocking things were discovered, the most prominent of which was the defendants' eagerness to confess their guilt. When the court conducted separate interrogations, Kamenev confessed that their conspiracy to commit terrorist acts was due to personal resentment towards Stalin and the desire to seize power. As for his personal animosity towards Stalin, it was actually due to Stalin's implementation of a certain socialist policy that proved successful. Kamenev also confessed to a far-reaching conspiracy, implicating the formal spokesperson for Soviet Russian foreign policy, Radek, and Bukharin, the editor-in-chief of Izvestia, the official propaganda organ of the Central Executive Committee. (Reuters dispatch, 23rd)

Trotsky's Indignant Remarks

Oslo, Norway. The Soviet anti-establishment leader Trotsky recently commented on the counter-revolutionary case fabricated by the current Soviet authorities, for which the Soviet authorities have sentenced people to death. Now, except for Lenin, who died long ago, and Stalin, who holds great power, the other five have been accused of using terrorist means and conspiring to harm the state. Tomsky has led the labor movement for the past thirty years and made outstanding contributions. He is one of the important leaders of the Soviet Union. Now, he has ended his life with a tragic end, which is regrettable. In short, Tomsky's suicide and the counter-revolutionary case fabricated in Moscow have very clear significance. What is the significance? That is, the traditional spirit and political program of the entire Communist Party have died halfway." (Havas dispatch, 24th)

Oslo, Norway. (Reuters dispatch, 24th)

Main Text of the Supreme Court Verdict

(Moscow) The main text of the verdict of the Military Collegium of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union regarding Zinoviev, Kamenev, and the other fourteen defendants is as follows:

"In the autumn of 1932, based on the order that Smirnov, the leader of the Trotskyist faction conducting secret work in the Soviet Union, received from Radek, the Trotskyist faction conducting secret work and the Zinovievist faction formed a 'Joint Center,' including Zinoviev, Kamenev, Yevdokimov, and Bakayev (representing the Zinoviev faction) and Smirnov, Termer-Teryan, and Fritz David (representing the Trotsky faction). The combination of this counter-revolutionary group was completed on the basis of implementing individual terrorist means against the leaders of the Soviet Communist Party and the Soviet government. Under the direct orders of Trotsky received by the Trotskyists in the 'Joint Center' through the defendants Smirnov, Goltzman, and Ter-Vaganyan, during this period (1932-1936), they concentrated their hostile activities against the Soviet government and the Soviet Communist Party, focusing on organizing terrorist acts against the leaders of the government and the party. The court has proven that this 'Joint Center,' under the direct command of Trotsky and Zinoviev, and through the Zinovievist terrorist members in Leningrad, Nikolaev, Kotorin, etc., organized and carried out the despicable assassination of Kirov, a member of the Presidium of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union and a member of the Central Committee of the Soviet Communist Party, on December 1, 1934.

"The Trotsky Center was not satisfied with the assassination of Kirov. It also prepared to carry out terrorist acts against Stalin, Voroshilov, Zhdanov, Kaganovich, Ordzhonikidze, Kosior, and Postyshev. According to the materials obtained by the court's investigation and the confessions of Zinoviev, Kamenev, Yevdokimov, Bakayev, Mirashkovsky, and Ter-Vaganyan, it has been proven that Trotsky abroad and Zinoviev in the country made efforts to accelerate the preparations for the assassination of Kirov. In order to accelerate the assassination of Kirov, Kamenev, carrying the order of the Trotskyist Joint Center, went to Leningrad in June 1934 to discuss with Yakovlev, one of the leaders of the Leningrad terrorist group, how to organize terrorist acts against Kirov. Yakovlev's case will be tried separately. The court also confirmed that Bakayev, carrying the order of the 'Joint Center,' also went to Leningrad in November 1934 to inquire of the terrorist member in that city, Nikolaev Kotorinov, how far the preparations for the assassination of Kirov had progressed. When the members of the group held secret meetings, Bakayev listened to the report of Leony Nikolaev, the assassin of Kirov, and, on behalf of the Trotskyist Joint Center, gave him and his accomplices practical instructions on how to organize the assassination of Kirov. According to these instructions, Nikolaev and his party carried out the assassination of Kirov on December 1, 1934.

"The court also proved that Bakayev, Reingold, and Ter-Vaganyan, in 1934, following the resolution of the 'Joint Center,' once plotted to assassinate Stalin. In order to ensure that this terrorist act planned by the 'Joint Center' would not fail, the center organized the so-called 'Moscow Terrorist Center' in Moscow in 1933, including Reingold, Pikel, and Ter-Vaganyan, and was under the direct guidance of Bakayev, a member of the 'Joint Center.' The 'Joint Center' assigned Bakayev to be responsible for the actual preparation and implementation of the assassination of Stalin and Kirov, while Ter-Vaganyan, a member of the 'Moscow Terrorist Center,' was assigned to organize terrorist acts against Voroshilov.

"Trotsky was not satisfied with directly commanding the 'Joint Center' to carry out terrorist acts against the leaders of the Soviet government and the Soviet Communist Party. During the period from 1932 to 1936, in order to achieve the same goal, he also systematically sent many terrorist members from abroad to the Soviet Union. In mid-November 1932, Trotsky sent Berman Yurin and Fritz David to the Soviet Union. When they set off, Trotsky personally instructed them on the methods of organizing the assassination of Stalin. In the same year, Trotsky also sent the terrorist Natan Lurie from Berlin to Moscow. After Lurie arrived, he colluded with Himmler (the current head of the Gestapo)'s confidant Franz Weitz, a secret agent of the Gestapo (German secret political police), to jointly prepare the assassination of Stalin, Voroshilov, Kaganovich, and Ordzhonikidze. At that time, Weitz posed as a foreign expert living in Moscow. After Weitz left Moscow in the winter of 1932, Natan Lurie and his terrorist members continued this terrorist activity, but in cooperation with Moses Lurie, who came to Moscow from Berlin in March 1933, also under Trotsky's order to accelerate the assassination work of Soviet government and Communist Party leaders. In 1934, at the construction site of the Chelyabinsk factory, Natan Lurie attempted to assassinate Kaganovich and Ordzhonikidze. Finally, on May 1, 1936, Natan Lurie, carrying Moses Lurie's order and with his prior consent, attempted to assassinate Zhdanov during the May Day parade in Leningrad.

"In the summer of 1935, Trotsky, through his son Sedov, sent the terrorist Orlov from Berlin to the Soviet Union. This person used a forged passport of the Republic of Honduras, which was obtained with the help of the Gestapo. Orlov obtained Trotsky's prior consent through Sedov. This incident should seek the assistance of the German secret police. After arriving in the Soviet Union, Orlov immediately established a connection with the counter-revolutionary terrorist members of the Trotskyist faction in Gorky City and prepared many terrorist members, ordering them to carry out the assassination of the Soviet government and the Soviet Communist Party leaders in Red Square in Moscow on May 1, 1936.

Page 10

"The court will further prove that, in addition to preparing terrorist acts against Stalin, Voroshilov, Zhdanov, Kaganovich, Ordzhonikidze, the Trotskyist terrorist center also carried out terrorist acts against Kosior and Postyshev through terrorist members in Ukraine. These Ukrainian terrorist members were under the guidance of the Trotskyist Mokshin, and their case will be tried separately.

"Therefore, the crimes of Zinoviev, Kamenev, Yevdokimov, Bakayev, Mirashkovsky, Ter-Vaganyan, and Smirnov have been proven, because they (A) organized the Trotskyist Joint Center, plotted to assassinate the leaders of the Soviet government and the Soviet Communist Party, (B) prepared and carried out the assassination of Kirov on December 1, 1934, through the secret terrorist members in Leningrad, Nikolaev, Kotorinov, etc., (C) organized many terrorist groups, preparing to assassinate Stalin, Voroshilov, Zhdanov, Kaganovich, Ordzhonikidze, Kosior, and Postyshev, violating Article 58, Clause 8, and Clause 11 of the Criminal Code of the Russian Socialist Federative Soviet Republic.

"Ter-Vaganyan, Reingold, Pikel, Goltzman, Fritz David, (Kruglyansky) Orlov, Berman, Yurin, and Moses Lurie are members of the Trotskyist counter-revolutionary secret terrorist organization, and actively participated in the preparation of the assassination of Party and state leaders such as Stalin. They are guilty of violating Articles 19, 58, 8, etc., and Articles 58-11, etc., of the Criminal Code of the Russian Socialist Federative Soviet Republic.

"Based on the above facts, the Military Collegium of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union sentences Zinoviev, Kamenev, Yevdokimov, Bakayev, Mirashkovsky, Ter-Vaganyan, Smirnov, Ter-Vaganyan, Reingold, Pikel, Goltzman, Fritz David, (Kruglyansky) Orlov, Berman, Yurin, Moses Lurie, and Natan Lurie to the highest punishment, namely execution by shooting, and all of their personal property should be confiscated. As for Trotsky and his son Sedov, who are now abroad, because the confessions of the defendants Smirnov, Goltzman, Ter-Vaganyan, Orlov, Fritz David, Paerzhro, Yurin, etc., and the materials of this case have proven that they directly prepared and personally directed the organization of terrorist acts against the leaders of the Soviet Communist Party and the anti-Soviet government in the Soviet Union, if they are found within the territory of the Soviet Union, they should be immediately arrested and handed over to the Military Collegium of the Supreme Court of the Soviet Union for trial." (TASS dispatch, 24th)

New Anglo-Egyptian Treaty to be Formally Signed Tomorrow; Egyptian Delegation Arrives in London, Receives Enthusiastic Welcome from Crowds

(London) The fully empowered Egyptian delegation, comprised of thirteen prominent figures, arrived in London last night. Their purpose is to formally sign the recently concluded Anglo-Egyptian treaty. All discord between Britain and the Egyptian Nationalist Party has been dispelled by the treaty’s conclusion. The Egyptian delegation is led by the current Prime Minister, General Nahas. The delegation includes twelve generals, three of whom previously served as Prime Ministers: namely, Muhammad Sidqi and Abdu'l-Fattah Yahya. Victoria Station was crowded with enthusiastic well-wishers last night, including many Egyptians residing in Britain. When British Foreign Secretary Eden stepped forward to shake hands with General Nahas, the crowd shouted, "Long live Anglo-Egyptian friendship!" The Anglo-Egyptian treaty is scheduled to be formally signed on Tuesday morning in the historically significant Locarno Room of the British Foreign Office. This new treaty supplements the Anglo-Egyptian treaty of 1922. While that treaty significantly advanced Egyptian independence, it still contained numerous reservations, such as the British right to station troops in Egypt, the future of the Sudanese government, the defense of the Suez Canal, and the consular jurisdiction over legal cases involving foreigners. These matters remained unresolved. Although the contents of the new treaty have not yet been officially released, the following outline is believed to be reliable: (1) The treaty constitutes an alliance and seeks amity between the two countries. (2) British troops will withdraw from Cairo and be stationed in Ismailia. (3) The defense of the country and the Suez Canal will ultimately be the responsibility of Egypt, but the number of British troops will not be reduced until the Egyptian army is sufficiently strong. (4) Egypt will construct military roads to facilitate rapid troop transport between the eastern and western parts of the country. (5) The British air force stationed in Egypt will be significantly increased, and new airfields may be built in Abu Qir and Ismailia. (6) Britain will establish an important naval base in Alexandria, and may also establish an army base there. Britain will pay rent for the occupied areas. (Reuters, 24th)

"Queen Mary" Breaks Speed Record; Returns from the US Faster than French Ship, Wins Blue Riband

(New York) The "Queen Mary" liner arrived at Ambrose Lightship at 4:12 AM (British Standard Time) this morning, taking four days, seven hours, and twelve minutes from her departure from Cherbourg. Her average speed was 30.01 nautical miles per hour. The French liner "Normandie" set the transatlantic speed record on her maiden voyage at four days, eleven hours, and forty-two minutes, averaging 29.94 nautical miles per hour. She departed from Cowes, a journey 50 miles longer than the "Queen Mary's." However, to win the Blue Riband for Atlantic crossings, the "Queen Mary" must surpass last year's "Normandie" east-to-west transatlantic speed record of 30.31 nautical miles per hour. This victory, for the west-to-east crossing, is, according to White Star Line, four hours and thirty minutes faster than the "Normandie's" record, with an average speed increase of 0.36 nautical miles per hour. (Reuters, 24th)

German Government Announces Arms Export Ban to Facilitate Neutrality Agreement on Spain; Seized Aircraft Case Seeks Satisfactory Resolution

(Berlin) The German government announced today that it is immediately banning the export of arms, ammunition, and other war materials to Spain. The German government is taking this step because the countries concerned have agreed in principle to participate in the neutrality agreement proposed by the French government. This ban has been communicated to the German government through diplomatic channels. The communication stated that the dispute between Berlin and Madrid regarding the seizure of a German aircraft by the Spanish authorities has not yet been resolved. The current ban does not affect the need to resolve this dispute. The German government hopes that other countries concerned will also implement this ban promptly without delay. (Reuters, 24th)

(Berlin) The German government informed France today that Fuehrer Hitler has issued an order prohibiting the shipment of munitions to Spain. This order is effective immediately. Officials also announced that the German cruiser "Köln," the torpedo boat "Seeadler," and the "Albatross" have returned to Germany from Spain. The pocket battleship "Deutschland" and the "Admiral Scheer," as well as two torpedo boats, will also return home once replacement warships arrive in Spain. This significantly eases the previously escalating international dispute. (National News Agency, 24th)

North China Japanese Consuls Conference Concludes; All Proposals Echo Army Demands; Naval Attachés Also Hold Meeting

Tianjin dispatch: The North China Japanese Consuls Conference convened at 9 AM on the 22nd at the Consul General's residence in the British concession of Tianjin. Ambassador Kawagoe served as the central figure. Participants included Foreign Ministry official Ota, acting Tianjin Consul General Tajiri, Consuls Kishi Ichi, Murakami, Taniguchi, Vice Consuls Nagai, Nishida, Jinan Consul General Arino, Qingdao Consul General Nishi Haruhiko, Zhangjiakou Consul General Nakane, Shanhaiguan Vice Consul Hara, Beijing Embassy Secretary Mutō Hanawa, Shanghai Embassy Secretaries Hoshino and Ogihara. Also attending were representatives from the China Prosperity Company, Kiyono, and the South Manchuria Railway Office, Ota, totaling over three thousand people. The meeting adjourned for lunch. The meeting participants then attended a banquet hosted by Naval Attaché to Tianjin, Colonel Kubota. Opinions regarding the two provinces overseas were exchanged during the banquet. The meeting continued at 2 PM and concluded at 6 PM. On the evening of the same day, Kawagoe hosted a banquet for the army and navy attachés at the public hall for mutual enjoyment. At 9 AM on the 23rd, the meeting continued at the same location. The meeting adjourned for lunch, and all matters were resolved by 5 PM, at which point the meeting was adjourned. The scope of the two-day discussions included: 1. Each consul's report on the current status of their work. 2. Foreign Ministry official Tian conveyed the ministry's views on the North China situation and economic issues. 3. Based on the Foreign Ministry telegram of the 19th, Kawagoe instructed the consuls on future work and diplomatic policy. 4. Discussion of measures to adapt to the North China situation. 5. Determination of specific plans for economic cooperation. 6. Expansion of police authority in North China, centered on Tianjin. 7. Expansion of the organizational structure of the Tianjin Consulate General, centered on the Tianjin Consul General. The first day focused on work reports and exchange of views on general issues. Official Ota, based on the Foreign Ministry's intention, elaborated on the results of his contact in Changchun, hoping that the North China diplomats would flexibly apply the unified economic diplomacy. Tianjin Vice Consul Nagai reported on his commercial survey materials as a reference for economic issues. In addition, special trade protection and tariff reduction were discussed for an extended period. The second day was devoted to drafting specific proposals for official Ota to take back to the country for reporting. Regarding the promotion of the realization of a clear-cut North China regime, Kawagoe provided opinions based on the meetings on the 17th and 21st. After deliberation, it was decided to accommodate the demands of the army side, take a consistent diplomatic approach, and encourage progress. After the meeting, on the evening of the 23rd, Kawagoe hosted the consuls at the Shikishima Hotel in the Japanese concession. On the morning of the 24th, he attended a high-ranking army and navy officer's meeting convened at the residence of Zhang Yuan, and was invited to a banquet by Zhang Zizhong at noon. At 11:30 PM, he left Tianjin by the Pingpu train to visit Han Fuju in Jinan to inquire about his attitude toward the North China situation. Arino Nishi Haruhiko accompanied him back to his post and spent a day in Jinan before going to Qingdao. On the 27th, he took a ship back to Shanghai. On the 28th, he convened the Central and South China Consuls Conference. Official Ota was scheduled to visit Song Zheyuan in Peiping on the 26th for a discussion, and would arrive in Shanghai by China Aviation flight on the 27th to attend the South China Consuls Conference.

Following the Three-Province Army, Navy, and Foreign Affairs Representatives Conference on the 21st, a system of separate discussions was adopted. The responsible persons from the three parties convened separate meetings to discuss matters related to their respective provinces for the study of the high-ranking officer's meeting on the 24th. In the Foreign Affairs aspect, the North China Consuls Conference was convened. In the Army aspect, Shadow Sazo and Hashimoto convened a military attaché conference at Zhang Yuan's residence at 9 AM on the 22nd. Participants included Matsumuro, Ōmoto, Imai, Hayama, Kōno, Ishino, Hosoki, Kuwahara, and dozens of military officers, including Wachi and Ikeda. Shadow Sazo reported on the views of the ministry. The proposals from the 22nd conference were reviewed, with those related to the army being considered separately. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM. In general, the parties decided to closely coordinate the establishment of economic and diplomatic policies for North China, with the embassy in the south and the garrison headquarters in the north as the centers of activity, echoing each other to avoid divergences in diplomatic steps. The responsibility for promoting the clarification of the North China regime was assigned to the military, with the embassy assisting in its implementation. Economic development was assigned to the embassy, with the military assisting in its implementation. In addition, the diplomatic and economic systems in North China would absolutely support each other to avoid conflicting forces that would hinder success. The hope for the Jicha authorities was to achieve genuine Sino-Japanese unity and local stability from within themselves. The abolition of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council and the general situation were discussed with the participation of Major Kumaō Ōhashi, a staff officer sent by the Kwantung Army. The resulting view was quite strengthened, recognizing that the abolition of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council was not yet timely. Great attention was paid to our central government's resolution of the Guangdong issue and the strengthening of the government's power. The joint meeting of high-ranking officers from all parties on the morning of the 24th used this intention as a base point. After discussion and passage, Lieutenant Colonel Shadow Sazo took the original draft to Jinan on the same night, then to Qingdao, and then to Shanghai to contact the North China military attachés.

As for the Naval Attachés Conference, it was convened at 1 PM on the 23rd at the Tianjin Naval Attaché's office in the Japanese concession, with Lieutenant Colonel Nakamura, a representative of the Navy Ministry, as the central figure. Colonel Kuwahara Shigetō, the Naval Attaché in Peiping, and Colonel Kubota of Tianjin attended. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM and resumed at 9 AM on the 24th, adjourning at noon. The scope of the agenda included: 1. Nakamura conveyed the intentions of the Navy Ministry. 2. Kubota and Kuwahara reported on the current status of their work. 3. Discussion of matters requiring cooperation on the development of the economy and the navy. 4. Issues related to the opening of ports in North China and the connection of the Tianjin-Tanggu tramway. 5. Expansion of the Navy's overseas organizations and the permanent stationing of ships at Tianjin Port. The results of the meeting were presented by Nakamura at the high-ranking officer's meeting on the afternoon of the same day for research and coordination with the Army and Foreign Affairs parties. On the 25th, he went to Peiping to investigate, stayed for several days, and returned to the country via the Northeast. (24th)

Mongol Puppet Bandit Army Prepares to Invade Sui on a Large Scale; Sui Army Reinforces Defenses in Taolin and Other Areas

Zhangjiakou dispatch: Puppet bandit Wang Ying went to Chahar North at the beginning of the month, gathered over a thousand bandits, and occupied Shangdu, intending to disturb Sui East. Wang bandit came to Zhangbei a few days ago and, in addition to contacting certain parties for arms, reorganized the bandits in Zhangbei to concentrate training. It is now reported that Wang bandit's contact with arms matters has been allowed by certain parties to supply Wang bandit. It is decided that around the 25th of this month, Wang bandit will leave Zhangbei for Shangdu and gather the troops of Li Shouxin, Zhang Haipeng, and De Wang, totaling approximately 26,000 people, and will invade Sui East on a large scale in early or mid-September. Currently, De Wang is extorting horses and levying grain from the people of various counties in Chahar North in preparation for war. Zhang Haipeng's troops are currently stationed near the city of Bin County, with approximately two thousand bandits. Today (21st), a person from Suiyuan stated that if the bandit army invades Sui, the Jin-Sui army is determined to use all its strength to strengthen defenses in Xinghe Taolin and other places. It is also reported that the bandit army of De Wang, etc., is mostly a rabble, and many of the Mongol soldiers are quite wealthy and will never be willing to sacrifice themselves on the battlefield.

Anhui Province Clears Scattered Bandit Groups; Provincial Government Formulates Pacification Plan

Anqing dispatch: Various groups of Red bandits in southern and western Anhui, as well as large groups of local bandits such as Chen Sanbazi and Fu Jiafa in northern Anhui, have all been successively wiped out, leaving only scattered small groups that gather and disperse unpredictably. The provincial government has formulated the following pacification plan for thorough suppression: (A) Divide the suppression areas and investigate the bandit situation in various places. Several suppression areas will be divided, and senior personnel will be assigned to unified command, regardless of regional boundaries, to conduct strict searches and suppressions. All bandits in the province will be eliminated within this year. (B) Divide the defense tasks. Security teams will assist garrison troops in guerrilla warfare, while the militia teams will be responsible for guarding. The provincial police and militia teams should strengthen blockades. Nearby garrison troops and security teams should also go to assist in the suppression. After the bandits retreat, they should jointly follow up and pursue them to inflict heavy damage. If the bandits' trail is lost, the militia teams should use their familiarity with the terrain to conduct in-depth searches. As soon as the bandits are found, the security teams or garrison troops should quickly rush to suppress them. (C) Compile and check the Baojia household registration system. Local areas will be responsible for carefully compiling and training the Baojia system, implementing joint security and joint responsibility, strictly checking household registrations, and interrogating travelers to ensure that local ruffians cannot gain a foothold to cut off their collusion and support, and to ensure that scattered bandits who are defeated cannot hide. Eliminate the source of bandits. (D) Complete the construction of blockhouse projects to prevent unexpected bandit attacks. Using fewer to defend against more, using leisure to await labor, and using disparate shapes can have great effects. The blockhouses can also isolate traffic and control the flow of bandits. If the bandits are gathered in one place, the existing blockhouses can be used to build trenches and connect them into a blockhouse line to encircle and block them, and then annihilate them in one fell swoop. The construction of blockhouses in various parts of the province has been completed. There is a deadline to complete the city defense and provincial defense. Anqing is the political center of the province and the key to the Beijing-Hankou transportation route. In times of emergency, the defense is particularly important. This year, it is planned to repair the original city walls, dredge the moat, gather the necessary troops, and dig outer moats along the ponds on the outer sides of the mountains and hills outside the city. Then, artillery positions will be set up at Qipan Mountain, Lion Mountain, and other places. At the same time, heavy machine gun emplacements will be constructed and machine guns will be placed along the important locations on the river banks of the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River to block the river surface with their firepower. As for the provincial defense, it is more necessary to quickly complete the preparations with the assistance of the central government. (August 23)

Kunshan: Grandeur of Zhouxiang Temple Fair

Zhouxiang Town in the sixth district of the county holds a grand temple fair every year on the sixth day of the seventh lunar month. This year, the farmers of various villages are silently praying for a good autumn harvest, so they are unusually excited and actively organizing the event. On the 22nd, all the villages burned incense and lit candles, paraded in procession, and displayed various colored lanterns, which were extremely dazzling. The villagers were elated all day long, as if drunk or enchanted. The farm boats were decorated with ribbons and performed various maneuvers in the river, competing for supremacy. The spectators on both banks were packed like sardines. The grandeur was rare. An old woman named Sun fell into the river by accident during a tense performance, but was rescued by the crowd. Fortunately, she revived, but she was foaming at the mouth. The villagers all believed that the deity had manifested, and all knelt and prayed, which was also quite laughable.

Jiading: Central School Vandalized

On the 23rd, Shen Youyi, a teacher who had been suspended from duty (for disobeying orders to attend summer school), and his brother Youkang, together with a dozen local ruffians, entered the school, surrounded the principal's office, and interrogated Principal Jin Guobao about why the Education Bureau's suspension order had been forwarded. Principal Jin replied that he was only following orders. Shen immediately resorted to violence, kicking and punching Jin, and destroying the equipment in the room. Jin has now petitioned the Education Bureau to forward the case to the county Public Security Bureau for the arrest and interrogation of the two Shens.

Two People Injured by Train

At around 9 PM on the 23rd, a local Shanghai-Xiang train on the Beijing-Shanghai line, traveling from Nanxiang to Jiangqiao station, struck two villagers who were crossing the railway in the dark without looking out. One was run over and had a foot severed. The injury was very serious and could be life-threatening. The other suffered minor foot injuries. Both were taken to Shanghai for treatment by the original train.

Wuxi: Collision Causes Fatal Accident

Jiankou, on the northern outskirts of the county, has a wide river surface and is a convenient place for Yonglu traffic. Ships come and go in an endless stream. The day before yesterday (23rd) at around 8 PM, Yan Xu, a housewife from a wonton shop in Sanliqiao, and Rongdi, a thirteen-year-old adopted daughter, were rowing a boat carrying samples from the Xisheng warehouse. While sailing through the area, a boat carrying incense approached. The two boats collided. Rongdi lost her footing and fell into the river, tragically drowning. When Rongdi's body was fished out, it was already beyond resuscitation.

Truth About Yu Lili's Accusation

Yu Lili (the little doll), the leading actress of the Shanghai opera in the Phoenix Hall of the Great World Amusement Park in Dongxin Road, outside the Guangfu Gate of the county, and her father, Yu Ruixiang, were secretly accused to the court of conspiring to murder. After two interrogations, due to the seriousness of the case, Yu Ruixiang was released on written bail of 5,000 yuan, but was later detained for lack of bail. As for the reason for the arrest of the little doll, it was rumored that the male corpse found with knife wounds under the Xadiang Bridge on the 13th of this month was Wu, a missing member of the troupe, causing Yu and others to be heavily suspected of murder. The inside story of the case has now come to light. Wu Piaoping, the missing Shanghai opera male actor, was found in Shanghai the other day. Wu Piaoping's original name was Zhang Zishi, age 40, living in Dachang Township, Shanghai. He received higher education and previously worked in the business and education sectors. He was always fascinated by Shanghai opera, and had a close friendship with Zhu Guodi, who currently performs Shanghai opera at the Great World in Shanghai. Later, the Shanghai Shanghai Opera Research Association was established, and he joined as a member and was hired as a secretary and director of the registration department. Therefore, he was very familiar with the leading actors of Shanghai opera. Since the opening of the Great World in the county, Wu was invited by Yang Liansheng to help in the opera team. All the little dolls and Shi Xiangyun were introduced and organized by Wu. Later, due to Shi Xiangyun listening to rumors and competing for the leading role, various disputes arose. Wu was blamed and left without saying goodbye on the evening of the 8th of this month, wearing a vest. He borrowed special funds from a friend in Suzhou and went to live at the Wu family in Shanghai's Dachang. On the morning of the 22nd, he took a steam bus back to Shanghai, went to Zhu Guodi's house in Beijings Road Feikangli to prepare travel expenses. Zhu then told him about the situation in Wuxi. At the same time, the mother of the little doll, Xu, entrusted her friend Wu Shutang to find him in Shanghai. He was found at Zhu Guobiao's house and immediately reported to the Shanghai Shanghai Opera Research Association. The association held an emergency meeting, recommending Changwu Zhu Xiaofeng, Wang Shaofeng, and Shu Zujun, carrying membership certificates, and together with Wu Piaoping, arrived in Wuxi from Shanghai at 4 AM on the previous day (23rd) and stayed at the First Hotel. Yesterday (24th), a complaint was written and reported to the District Court at 8 AM. The judge Shen opened the court for interrogation. As a result, Yu Ruixiang was ordered to change to ordinary bail, and Shi Shaoqing and Yan Chungen each added a written bail of six yuan. Yang Liansheng was returned to prison for the opium case, and the others were ordered to return home pending review. At this point, the so-called sex scandal that had caused a storm in the city came to an end.

Changshu: Rice Fields in Four Townships Damaged by Insects

It is reported that rice fields in other provinces have a bumper harvest this year. However, in the four townships of Changshu, the autumn harvest has been greatly reduced due to insect damage. The weather was unusually hot when the rice seedlings were transplanted this summer. During the hot season, it suddenly turned cool again. As a result, the rice crops did not develop well. In the western townships, black ear disease (commonly known as "heart extraction") has occurred and is spreading rapidly. The agricultural extension institute has telegraphed the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute, requesting them to send personnel to Changshu to investigate and find ways to save the crops.

Changzhou: Silkworm Cocoon Businesses Certified in Silkworm Area

The Wuyi Silkworm Improvement Area distributed autumn silkworm seeds this term, with a total of 90,000 sheets distributed in various villages. Currently, a large number of autumn silkworms have been harvested, and the early batch has already reached the 1-2 instar feeding stage. The improvement area has separately collected statistics on qualified cocoon businesses and those that have not opened in three years. After verification, 35 businesses, including Hongtaichang and Tongfengzhai, have been certified and registered. As the date of the full autumn harvest is approaching, a list is specially reported to the Provincial Sericulture Improvement Management Committee for review and filing.

Hangzhou: Method for Stacking Salt

Zhang Zhongli, Director of the Lianghai Salt Affairs Tax Bureau, who was previously summoned to Shanghai by the General Office of Salt Affairs Inspection in Feng, to inquire about the Daisan salt farmers' rebellion, has completed his official duties and returned to Hangzhou. According to Zhang's discussion with reporters: (A) Regarding the method for stacking salt, the Engineering Office will, in conjunction with local authorities, designate the location of the stacking base, delineate the scope, and organize a council to evaluate the price of the stacking base. The price of the land will be paid to the owners at any time. The time for paying the salt will be from sunrise to sunset. (B) Regarding the method of changing the color of fishing salt, the pigment will be issued by the government, the fish salt brick storage will be built by the government, the baskets and carrying poles will be purchased by the government, and a request will be made to banking groups and financial groups to provide loans to relieve the fishermen.

Jiaxing: Distribution of Autumn Silkworm Eggs

The Jiaxing County Sericulture Improvement Zone has decided to release a total of 50,000 sheets of autumn silkworm eggs this year. However, due to the large number of silkworm eggs in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, there is a general shortage, resulting in a significant shortfall in the estimated quantity. The Zhejiang Unified Control Council has specifically stipulated that the distribution will be at 80% to 90% of the determined number of eggs. Jiaxing can only distribute 36,000 sheets. Zheng Genquan, the director of the zone, believing that farmers are idle in the autumn and that raising autumn silkworms can provide some additional income, personally went to Suzhou, Zhenjiang, and other places to negotiate with various egg production farms and added 7,000 sheets from the two locations. Therefore, the distribution can be at 90% of the determined number. A large batch of silkworm eggs has now arrived in He, and distribution began successively on the 24th.

Wuhu: Dachang Match Factory

Wuhu is the commercial center of Anhui Province. In recent years, it has been affected by the bankruptcy of the rural economy, and the market is quite sluggish. Since the successive opening of the Jiangnan, Huainan, and other railways and various highways, coupled with the abundant harvests of agricultural products in Anhui Province in both spring and autumn, Wuhu has become the tail end of transportation and sales, and the atmosphere is thriving. All sectors of the party and government, as well as local gentry, are implementing the industrial plan set by the late Sun Yat-sen, with Wuhu as an industrial zone, and are now恪遵the late leader's instruction to engage in resumption of work. Factories such as textile mills and match factories are all in the planning stage. According to recent reports, although there is a saying that a joint production and sales system will be implemented in the match industry, the Dachang Match Factory was leased by the Shanghai Dachina Match Factory in the spring of the 20th year of the Republic of China, first for five years and then renewed for another five years. However, Dachina only leased but did not operate, and the Dachang Factory was restricted by the contract. It had to wait until the lease expired on March 14 of this year before negotiating to terminate the contract. Therefore, on December 24 of the previous year, it submitted a request to both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry to take back the factory and operate it independently upon the expiration of the lease. The Ministry of Industry approved the request. At that time, the government did not impose restrictions on the match industry, and the so-called "Match Production and Sales Joint Operation Association Regulations" had not yet been approved and promulgated. Dachang's request was made earlier and should not be bound by it. This special situation must be appealed for relief. It is hoped that the government will take into account the facts, be fair and reasonable, and resolve the matter in order to prevent disputes.

Taizhou: Intercepting Smuggling Ships

The Silk, Lishi, and Shitang areas of Wenling are located on the coast, and smuggling is rampant. At midnight on the 16th, Chen Qifu, a local unscrupulous merchant, shipped another batch of smuggled goods from Taiwan, fully loaded on a large merchant ship, including white sugar and fertilizer. The ship sailed through Cheguan and stopped at the Shatao waters to entrust someone to sell and transport the goods. Due to lack of secrecy, Wu Liqing and Zhu Rongshou, local ruffians, learned of it. They immediately took up arms and led a group of people to board the ship and seize the goods. Later, Luo, the chief of the Houxiang bao, and Lin, a bao member, mediated. Chen Qifu was willing to pay 500 yuan in national currency to release the ship and sail it to the Diaobenglongzui waters. He wrote a receipt and set a deadline for the following day (the 17th) to pay the money. Later, because the cash could not be raised and the goods could not be unloaded, the incident was learned by the captain of the Shangmashishi Guard Team. He immediately reported to the team headquarters and dispatched troops to investigate and seize the ship. The incident was reported to the county government for instructions.

Local News

The Longhai Railway Bureau Hosted a Tour Yesterday to View New Steel Cars: Purchased a Total of 49 Cars at a Price of Three Million, with Equipment and Layout Superior to All Other Railways

The Longhai Railway Bureau ordered 49 new steel cars from Belgium. After the second batch of 13 cars was transported to Shanghai, it entrusted the Wusong Machine Factory of the Lianglu Bureau to complete the assembly. Yesterday afternoon, from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM, it hosted a tour for people from all walks of life. The new cars will depart at 8:00 PM that evening, taking the Jinghu and Jinpu railways and transferring to the Longhai Railway to join the operation. The details are recorded as follows:

Hosted Tour

The Longhai Railway Bureau hosted a tour for people from all walks of life at the First Platform of the North Station of the Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Bureau yesterday afternoon from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM. A total of more than 300 people attended, including Huang Boqiao, Yan Fang, Lin Jinyu, representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, various shipping companies, and reporters from various newspapers. Yin Saidi Zhong, Director of the Longhai Railway Shanghai Liaison Office, and others cordially greeted the guests and accompanied them on a tour of the internal equipment of the new cars, and provided tea and refreshments. People from all walks of life praised the new steel cars.

New Car Cost

The Longhai Railway Bureau ordered new steel cars from La Brugeoise et Nicaise et Delcuve S. Cp. of Belgium, introduced by the Belgian Silver Company, for a total of 49 cars, including 5 first-class sleeping cars, 7 second-class sleeping cars, 5 first-class dining cars, 1 lounge car, 5 second and third-class combined cars, 15 third-class passenger cars, 5 baggage cars, and 5 postal cars, for a total cost of 3 million yuan. After the first batch of new cars was transported to China and assembled, it has been allocated to the Longhai Line for use. The second batch (i.e., the tour hosted yesterday) of 13 new cars has been fully configured. The third and fourth batches of new cars are also in the process of shipping and construction. The new cars are 21 meters long, the car body is 18 meters and 98 centimeters long, and the weight of the first and second-class sleeping cars is 45 tons, the first-class dining cars and lounge cars weigh 46 tons, and the second and third-class combined cars and third-class passenger cars weigh 43 tons.

Structural Features

All parts inside and outside the cars are made of steel plates. The bumpers at both ends of the cars are also made of steel. The structure is extremely strong and can resist the pulling force of 100 tons of trailers. Even in the event of an accident, it can provide passengers with the highest level of safety, and the weight of the car body has not increased. The outer walls of the car body are painted in light green, which is bright and flat, and there are no nail heads protruding. The inner walls are fitted with teak panels to prevent the intrusion of heat and cold. The steps for getting on and off the car retract into the car, and are covered with a cover plate. The car door must be opened first, and then the cover plate can be opened before getting on and off, which is not only elegant but also safe. The two cars are closely connected to each other, and it is very stable to pass through them.

Exquisite Layout

The berths in the cars are arranged using scientific methods. The first-class sleeping car has eight bedrooms. The upper berth is parallel to the car window, and the lower berth is perpendicular to the car window. The upper and lower berths are in a B-shaped position. The upper berth can be climbed with a steel ladder and is close to the top of the car without leaving any traces. When the lower berth is not in use, it can be used as a seat. In addition, there is a small table and a sofa chair. Between every two bedrooms, each room has two upper and lower berths, which can be folded freely. In the middle of the car, there is a large washroom that can accommodate four people washing at the same time. The first-class dining car is divided into three parts: dining room, living room, and kitchen. The dining room has four tables for four people and four tables for two people, which can accommodate 24 people dining at the same time. The living room has four tables for two people and two movable folding tables, which can be moved at will. The car windows are wide, and passengers can enjoy the scenery while dining. The lounge car is divided into three parts: living room, bedroom, and kitchen. The layout is slightly the same as the first-class sleeping car. The second and third-class combined car is divided into two parts: second-class and third-class seats. In the second-class seats, there are 13 double rattan chairs, with wide seats and backs that are appropriately inclined. The palm cushions and springs are moderately soft and hard. The layout of the third-class seats is the same as that of the third-class passenger car. The characteristic of the third-class passenger car is that there are only 84 seats in a 21-meter-long car, the width of the chair surface reaches 52 mm, and the empty distance between the chairs is also 525 mm. Even when the seats are fully occupied, there is also a weapon room for the armed escort team police.

Sanitary Equipment

In addition to the safety equipment (such as wind brakes, brake shoes, automatic adjusters, etc.) and the lounge car equipped with a氏暖汽 and a hot water stove, all the facilities for passengers and various sanitary equipment are available in each car and are of the latest style. The quilts, curtains, and miscellaneous items in the car are specially made by this railway to increase the comfort and interest of passengers.

Northbound Last Night

According to Chen Shouzhong, director of the Longhai Railway Shanghai Liaison Office, the second batch of new steel cars has been assembled and painted. Explanation of the Method for Electing Medical and Pharmaceutical Professionals as Candidates

The Municipal Medical Association previously learned that the election of candidates by the Lawyers Association should be handled by the Standing Committee. The association is also a committee-based organization. It is doubtful whether it should also be handled according to the example in the future when electing candidates. Therefore, it submitted a request to the Municipal National Assembly Representative Election Exchange for explanation. The Exchange replied that the reason why the Lawyers Association stipulates that candidates should be elected by the Standing Committee is that the Lawyers Associations in various places are all president-based, while Shanghai is the only one that is committee-based. The Medical Association was originally committee-based, and it can still follow the regulations and the Executive Committee can be the elector for the candidate of the medical and health group. It is reported that a reply has been sent to inform them.

The Yanpu Godown Warehouse is Building a Water Defense Project, which will be Fully Completed Within Days, and there will be no More Flooding Worries in the Future

The steamship companies, banks, godowns, and warehouses along the Yanpu River in this city are facing the arrival of the autumn flood season. When the tide rises in the Huangpu River, the goods piled up on the bottom floor of the godowns and warehouses will inevitably be flooded. In order to prevent this from happening, they have notified the cargo owners to quickly retrieve their goods, otherwise they will be responsible for the moving expenses. According to a reporter from the Industrial News Agency, the goods on the bottom floor of the various godowns and warehouses along the Yanpu River have been retrieved by the cargo owners, and some have been moved to higher floors. Workers have been hired to build cement and other defense projects around the outside of the godowns and warehouses. The project will be fully completed within days. It is reported that if the Huangpu River floods in the future, the various godowns and warehouses will be unaffected.

Ten Million in Cash Shipped from Hankou to Shanghai: 600,000 Arrived on Saturday, 9.4 Million Arrived Yesterday

At the beginning of the currency reform last year, the silver stored in this city was shipped to Hankou and other places for storage in order to comply with the financial authorities' purpose of dispersing silver in various places. Now, because it is no longer necessary to store it in other ports, it has been ordered to ship the silver stored in Hankou back to Shanghai. Since last Saturday, 600,000 yuan has been loaded and shipped to Shanghai. Now, another 9.4 million yuan in silver, divided into 1,880 boxes, has been shipped directly to Shanghai from Hankou on a special riverboat. It arrived safely in Shanghai yesterday afternoon and was unloaded at the designated wharf. It was then stored in a certain bank's warehouse. Together with the 600,000 yuan that arrived in Shanghai on Saturday, the total amount is exactly 10 million yuan.

Page 13

Joint Announcement from the Ministries of Finance and Railways: Reorganization of the Longhai Railway, Methods for Repaying Principal and Interest, Reducing Interest by Approximately 15,000,000 Yuan; Additionally, Two Belgian-Dutch Advances Also Reorganized, and a Jointly Formed Fund Management Committee Will Be Responsible for Custody

Reorganization Process

Regarding the Ministry of Railways' reorganization of the Longhai Railway's debts, according to Central News Agency reporters' inquiries, since the first year of the Republic of China, foreign debts were successively borrowed from Belgium, France, and the Netherlands for construction. During the European War and due to domestic turmoil, the borrowed funds could not be fully issued as bonds. Subsequently, loans were repeatedly taken from Belgian and Dutch companies. However, since the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, principal and interest payments have been overdue. As of now, the accumulated principal is approximately 150,000,000 yuan, and the interest is approximately 100,000,000 yuan, totaling approximately 150,000,000 yuan in national currency. In recent years, representatives of the Belgian company have repeatedly urged a reorganization, but due to the incomplete construction of the railway, insufficient revenue, and the massive debt, the divergent opinions prevented any agreement from being reached. Recently, after our government announced the reorganization plans for the Tianjin-Pukou and Daqing Railways, the Belgian company representatives requested reorganization based on the same precedent. The Belgian, French, and Dutch ambassadors repeatedly protested to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Railways, urging a resolution. To maintain creditworthiness, our government sincerely negotiated a reorganization plan with the Belgian banking syndicate. After repeated discussions lasting nearly half a year, and overcoming numerous twists and turns, an agreement was finally reached. The reduction in interest, including past accrued interest and interest reduction until the start of principal repayment, amounts to approximately 15,000,000 yuan. This was achieved through the sincere cooperation of the Belgian, French, and Dutch parties. The detailed plan was announced yesterday by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Railways (see below). In addition, two Belgian-Dutch advances have also been reorganized. When the above reorganization plan is implemented, a fund management committee will be formed by the two banks and representatives of the bondholders, following the example of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, to be responsible for custody in order to ensure credibility. The agreed-upon arrangements for reorganizing the Longhai Railway debts have been approved by the 271st meeting of the Executive Yuan, then passed by the 19th meeting of the Central Political Committee, and subsequently by the National Government in Instruction No. 81 on August 18th of this year.

Announcement Content

The Minister of Finance and the Minister of Railways issued the following announcement yesterday to restore the repayment of principal and interest for the following loans of the Longhai Railway: (1) The 1913 £4,000,000 British gold 9% loan; (2) The 1920-1923 30,750,000 Guilder Dutch currency 8% short-term bonds; (3) The 1920-1921 and 1923 137,743,000 Franc Belgian currency 8% short-term bonds; (4) The 1924 5,000,000 Yuan Chinese currency 8% short-term public bonds; (5) The 1925 11,250,000 Franc French currency 8% short-term bonds issued to repay the 1919 loan. (1) Starting from July 1, 1936, the interest rate will be 1.5% in the first year, increasing by 0.5% each year until it reaches 4% in 1941-1942. Afterwards, the interest rate will be fixed at 4%. The interest for the first five years will be paid at the end of each fiscal year, and then 2% interest will be paid on January 1st and July 1st of each year. (2) Starting from July 1, 1947, a fixed annual amount will be used to repay both principal and interest, with a maximum repayment period of 35 years. The annual amount will be used to pay interest first, with the remaining amount used for principal repayment. If the bond price is equal to or higher than the face value, the principal will be repaid through a lottery system. If the bond price is lower than the face value, the loan manager will consult with the Chinese government's representative to purchase the bonds on the market. If the bonds cannot be purchased on the market, the loan manager will publish advertisements to solicit bids, purchasing from those offering the lowest price. Regardless of whether the bonds are repaid through a lottery or purchased on the market, the total amount allocated for principal repayment each year will be fully utilized. Regarding the above five types of loans, the Chinese government has the right to provide advance notice of early repayment each time principal is repaid. (3) All the above principal and interest payments should be prioritized from the operating profits of the Xi'an to Luoyang and Kaifeng to Haikou sections. After the 1903 loans and advances for the Kaifeng to Luoyang (i.e., Bianluo) section are repaid and that line is incorporated into the Longhai Railway, the surplus at that time will be transferred to the above-mentioned debt repayment fund. (4) All overdue interest before July 1, 1936, is completely waived. (5) Bondholders who accept these terms should submit their bonds to the loan manager, who will affix a stamp and attach new interest coupons. All foreign taxes on the interest coupons and principal shall be borne by the bondholders. The above plan is the result of lengthy discussions between the Chinese government and the bondholder representatives. Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Railways stated that the railway authorities will refer to the provisions of each loan contract to seek ways to improve railway administration, so that both the Chinese government and the bondholders can benefit.

Municipal Knitting Industry: Measures to Prevent Smuggling

The Shanghai Municipal Knitting Industry Association, in order to prevent smuggling and safeguard the legitimate sales of goods, has announced the following key points to the industry in accordance with the regulations for inspecting smuggling: (1) Registration: All industry members in the city should report to the association the accurate quantities of their existing goods and materials, along with their tax documents for the raw materials, immediately for registration. The deadline for this registration is August 31st. (2) Reporting: After completing the above registration procedures, all new incoming goods and materials must be reported to the association promptly. At the end of each month, a list of sales and usage for the entire month must be reported to the association. (3) Obtaining Certificates: Products from city industry members that have been registered and verified by the association, and are deemed without suspicion, can apply to the association for the issuance of certificates for transportation to various locations, for identification purposes, to avoid misunderstandings and detentions.

Agricultural Development Bureau: Decision to Establish Next Month, Working Capital Shared by Banking Syndicate

The Agricultural Development Bureau, jointly organized by the Ministry of Industries and various banks, is scheduled to convene a board meeting next month to announce its establishment. Regarding the bureau's working capital, it has been decided that the participating banks will jointly form a banking syndicate to handle loans. Inland Waterways Shipping Association Letters Customs: Discussing Methods for Small Steamer Towing, Presenting Difficulties of Changing to Double-Row Towing, Maintaining the Three Methods of the Former Harbour Master

The Shanghai Inland Waterways Shipping Association sent a letter yesterday to the Harbour Master of the Jianghai Customs, stating: Regarding Harbour Master's Notice No. 15735 of July 20th of this year, concerning the change of methods for small steamers towing vessels between the Suzhou Creek mouth and the Jiangnan Shipyard wharf, instructing that all members be informed and comply, etc. The association considers this a technical navigation issue, greatly related to the duties performed by crew members, and especially significant to the safety of small steamer navigation. Therefore, the association's executive committee conducted detailed research, on-site surveys, and also consulted the Shanghai branch of the Chinese Seamen's Union to seek opinions. The conclusions are listed as follows: (1) The passenger ships towed by small steamers in Shanghai Port can be divided into three categories: 1. Company ships carrying passengers; 2. Wuxi fast boats; 3. Tow barges carrying cargo. Among the tow barges carrying cargo, there are many types and different formats. The ships towed by small steamers cover almost all types. It is difficult to arrange these ships, with varying lengths and heights, into double rows for towing. Even in fast-flowing currents, double-row navigation would be more dangerous. Single-row navigation can be determined. (2) Ordinary cargo ships relying on sails and oars for propulsion still require hiring another steamer to tow them in the turbulent currents of the Huangpu River. Small steamers towing various vessels, whether carrying passengers or cargo, do not have oars. If, to avoid the danger of changing to double-row towing, they are required to tow in one trip, it would not only hinder navigation time but also be difficult to implement in practice. (3) During ebb tide, the water flowing out of the Suzhou Creek mouth is turbulent, making it impossible to change to double-row navigation. (4) When entering the Suzhou Creek mouth, dismantling the double row into a single row during high tide is very likely to cause collisions with the park embankment, posing a significant danger. (5) There are many ships docked in the Suzhou Creek mouth area. Double-row towing can easily obstruct port traffic. (6) According to the actual survey conducted by the association, for small steamers with a gross tonnage of 30 tons or more, whether during high or low tide, towing six barges out of the Suzhou Creek mouth can be handled with ease. The above are all facts. Based on the findings of the research, the changes made by your esteemed Harbour Master to the small steamer towing methods may not reduce the dangers on the river surface or protect the safety of vessels, and are not beneficial. Regarding the management of traffic in the narrow and congested section of the Lujiazui Bay, the association received Notice No. 14535 from the former Harbour Master, Mr. Le Tintin, on August 3, 1933, stipulating three regulations regarding the route of small steamers. Since the implementation of the above three methods to this day, the dangers of navigation have indeed been greatly reduced. These methods, suitable for managing port administration and facilitating vessel navigation, should still be allowed to be retained. The association is deeply grateful for your esteemed Harbour Master's enthusiasm in protecting the safety of vessels. We have presented a detailed letter listing the difficulties of changing to double-row towing and the fact that it does not help protect the safety of small steamers. We sincerely hope that your esteemed Harbour Master will reconsider to achieve a better solution and avoid implementation difficulties. With sincere regards, to Harbour Master Tepeike of the Harbour Affairs Department.

Banking Sector Assistance

Loans will also be sought from the Shanghai-Wuhan banking sector. The China Bank, the China Agricultural Loan Syndicate, and others, have designated loans of 4,000,000 yuan for agricultural loans in more than 30 counties. The Director of Finance of the province has come to Shanghai to negotiate and sign a contract. The construction of warehouses in various counties of the province has made progress and is scheduled to be fully completed next month. The government is conducting detailed research on issues such as the prohibition of wheat exports. The Flour and Grain Associations have not yet received approval from the ministry. The claim that Chinese merchants are purchasing foreign wheat is not confirmed. As for the price of Persian foreign rice, it is 6.5 yuan per dan (a unit of weight), which is roughly the same as the price of our country's wheat. However, only sample rice has been seen, and no transactions have been made.

National Association for the Prevention of Smuggling: Approves Operating Rules, Divided into Twelve Articles and Four Sections

The National Association for the Prevention of Smuggling approved the following operating rules of the association at its second standing committee meeting: Article 1: These rules are formulated in accordance with Article 10 of the association's organizational outline. Article 2: In addition to the seven standing committee members who handle daily affairs, the association is divided into four sections: General Affairs, Intelligence, Organization, and Statistics, with the following responsibilities: (1) General Affairs Section: Matters related to documents, accounting, communication, publicity, and other matters not belonging to other sections. (2) Intelligence Section: Matters related to investigation and communication. (3) Organization Section: Matters related to the organization of anti-smuggling associations in various regions and the review of articles of association. (4) Statistics Section: Matters related to the registration of anti-smuggling associations, commodity stores, and investigation of smuggled goods in various regions. Article 3: Each section shall have one director and one deputy director who are responsible for managing the affairs of the section. Article 4: The association shall have one secretary who, under the direction of the standing committee, manages the drafting, receiving, sending, and safekeeping of the association's documents. Article 5: The association shall have several staff members who, under the direction of the standing committee, section directors, and the secretary, handle various matters. Article 6: The association's documents must be signed by at least three standing committee members before they can be issued. Article 7: The association's office hours are from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM daily. Offices are closed on Sundays and holidays. Article 8: Section directors and the secretary may attend the standing committee meetings. Article 9: The association's financial income and expenditure shall be prepared monthly by the general affairs section and reported to the standing committee meeting for review and publication. Article 10: The association's work progress shall be prepared by the secretary with the assistance of the staff and sent to each member monthly. Article 11: The association's office is located in the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Article 12: These rules shall be implemented upon approval by the association's committee meeting, and the same applies to any amendments.

Income Tax: Questions on Implementation Rules, The "Debt" Character in Article 7 of Government Bonds is Likely Mistaken. Shen Liren Submits to Chief Gao for Instructions

Xinxin News Agency reports that the "debt" character in "government bonds debt" in Article 7 of the Income Tax Implementation Rules has caused public confusion, with some suspecting it to be a mistake for the "accumulation" character of "accumulation fund." A single character's difference is of great importance. Accountant Shen Liren has specifically sent a letter to Chief Gao of the Direct Tax Preparatory Office for clarification. His original letter stated: (Omitted above) The Income Tax Implementation Rules were published in various newspapers the other day. Article 7 states, "The term 'capital' refers to the paid-up share capital of a company or the actual capital invested by other organizations. Those with government bonds, can calculate one-third of their total amount into the capital." The "debt" character of "government bonds" is often confused with the "accumulation" character of "accumulation fund." The meanings of the two are different, and they also have a large impact on the interpretation of the word "capital" and the calculation of income. A single character's difference seems significant. Ordinary mistakes are insignificant, but in this article, it is very important. Therefore, I respectfully submit this for clarification.

Renji Hospital: July Report

Renji Hospital's July report states: Number of outpatient visits: 17,177; Number of new hospital admissions: 385; Number of inpatient days: 6,702; Average number of people provided with meals per month: 490; Male suicides: 57 cases; Female suicides: 62 cases; Emergency surgeries: 396 cases; Emergency surgeries for factory accidents: 45 cases; Patients sent by the British Concession Police: 470; Patients sent by the French Concession Police: 72; Deliveries: 20 cases. Overall, the statistics for July are consistent with past experience. The summer months show a surge, with outpatient and inpatient numbers increasing by over 10% compared to the previous month. Emergency surgeries also increased by approximately 20%. The increase in female suicides is a particularly tragic feature of July. There were 62 suicide cases, an increase of no less than 25% compared to the 48 cases in June. The common method of suicide is overdosing on opium, which is now easily obtainable and inexpensive. In 12 out of the 62 suicide cases, death occurred. Currently, only 50 cents can buy enough opium to kill a woman with a normal constitution. It is hoped that the authorities will make every effort to make it more difficult for the public to obtain opium. In July, there was a particularly pitiful patient who came to the hospital. The patient was a young man in his twenties from Nanjing, who had to have both arms and one leg amputated due to the spread of a lung infection. The outcome of this surgery, given the current difficult circumstances, is very good. It is planned to fit him with two prosthetic hands so that he can still earn a living when he leaves the hospital. The fitting of these prosthetic hands is free of charge. This is thanks to a generous donation from a famous Englishman in Shanghai, which is specifically for this purpose. However, this Englishman does not want his name to be publicized.

Shanghai-Ningbo Line Steamers Reduce Miscellaneous Grain Freight Rates: China Merchants and Others Decide to Implement in Order to Compete with Private Vessels

This port's China Merchants, Ning Shao, San Bei, Swire, and other four shipping companies, in order to compete with private shipping for freight, have specially reduced the freight rates for miscellaneous grains on the Shanghai-Ningbo line. Our news correspondent has investigated and reported the situation as follows:

Private Vessels Competing for Transport

Recently, because private vessels have been actively registering with the customs, they are able to clear customs and transport goods in the same way as steamers, and have therefore become quite developed. This is especially true for the close Shanghai-Ningbo route, where there are many private vessels traveling back and forth. These private vessels all have a considerable history, so they have a good reputation with merchants. Furthermore, private vessels have limited expenses and simple operations, so their prices for transporting passengers and goods are lower than those of steamers. Although the delivery time is slower than that of steamers, merchants are generally calculating based on the freight costs, and speed is secondary. As a result, the freight business of steamers is greatly threatened. The impact is even more pronounced on the Shanghai-Ningbo route, which is a near-sea route.

Reducing Freight Rates

This port's China Merchants, Ning Shao, San Bei, Swire, and other four shipping companies, therefore, convened a meeting some time ago. As a result, they decided to reduce the freight rates for miscellaneous grains on the Shanghai-Ningbo line. The freight rate for soybeans and rice will be reduced from 36 cents per hectoliter to 32 cents, with a further 20% discount. The freight rate for wheat flour will be reduced from 11 cents per bag to 10 cents, in order to compete with private vessels. A notice has been sent to Shanghai and Ningbo merchants and firms, stating that this will be implemented immediately to show their preferential treatment.

Bohai Bay Yellow River Estuary: Patrol Vessels Discover Shallow Water; Customs' Hua Xing Warship Discovers Sunken Ship in Dalian Bay Channel

The Hydrographic Office of this port has issued two notices regarding the discovery of shallow water in the Bohai Bay Yellow River estuary, and the discovery of a sunken ship in the Dalian Bay channel. All vessels are instructed to pay attention. The notices are recorded below:

Discovery of Shallow Water

Notice No. 197 states: Shallow water has been discovered near the Bohai Bay Yellow River estuary. (1) Position: East longitude 118 degrees 38 minutes 15 seconds, north latitude 38 degrees 11 minutes 45 seconds. (2) Description: It is reported that a depth of only six feet (1.83 meters) has been found at the above position. (3) Reporting agency: Customs patrol vessel "Hua Xing".

Discovery of a Sunken Ship

Notice No. 198 states: A sunken ship has been discovered in the Dalian Bay channel. (1) Position: 167 degrees from the Fei Cai Tuo Zi triangulation point, a distance of 2.05 chains (every 10 chains equals 1 nautical mile), which is approximately east longitude 121 degrees 52 minutes, north latitude 38 degrees 57 minutes. (2) Current state: A sunken ship is exposed above the water surface at low tide. (3) Description: The symbol for "sunken ship exposed at low tide" should be added to the chart at this location.

Dr. Chen Cheng Found Not Guilty: Forensic Examination Confirms Diagnosis Was Correct

Chen Cheng, director of Pu'an Hospital on Fair Road in Hongkou and head of surgery at Renji Hospital, was sued in the First Special District Court by a woman, Madam Ma Dong, for causing the death of her son, Ma Laoda, due to professional negligence. The court had repeatedly summoned Chen and ordered the submission of Chen's diagnosis and other documents to the Forensic Institute for examination. This has been reported in this newspaper multiple times. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide held a continued hearing in the First Criminal Court and released the report from the Forensic Institute, which stated that the results of the examination showed that Chen's diagnosis was correct and that this type of treatment was necessary. The death of Ma Laoda was actually due to physical weakness and poison in his stomach entering the heart, and Chen's surgery was not inappropriate. After ordering the start of arguments, the court immediately announced the judgment: Chen Cheng was found not guilty.

Follow-up Report on Fire in Pudong: Seventy or Eighty Shacks Destroyed; Victims Homeless

At 1:10 AM yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out in a small tobacco and paper shop opened by Bian Guangzhi, a Taizhou native, in a shack at No. 2 behind the Laiyi Taikoo Huatung Warehouse in Pudong. Because the thatched house was flammable, the fire quickly spread. The police were reported to the Pudong Sub-Bureau, and Director Zhang telegraphed the Pudong District Fire Brigade, the Yangjing Town Fire Brigade, and others, who rushed to the scene with pump trucks to put out the fire. After more than an hour of firefighters' efforts, the fire was extinguished. A total of 70 or 80 thatched shacks were destroyed, as well as two tiled houses and eight partially burned tiled houses. The fire area was quite large. The victims were generally immigrants from Jiangbei, and they were all homeless for a time, their cries filling the air, a very miserable sight. Yesterday afternoon, those with a little financial strength had already rebuilt new thatched shacks to live in. By evening, about a dozen had been built.

Female Tea Server Convicted of Theft: 30 Days Detention, Suspended Sentence

Wang Huangying, a female tea server at Tian Yunlou Cinema No. 9 in the Wing On Company on Nanjing Road, originally from Wuxi, is a young woman of twenty. A man named Lou Heqing, residing at No. 44, Tai'an Lane, Tiantong Road, often went to the cinema to watch plays, and Wang would serve him tea. They became acquainted and gradually intimate. One Saturday evening, Lou went again, and Wang served him with particular enthusiasm. When Lou was about to leave, he took out his wallet to pay for the tea, and Wang took the opportunity to snatch five yuan in legal tender, leading to a conflict. Detective Wu Qilan of the Lao Zha Police Station arrested Wang. Head Detective Yan interrogated Wang, but she repeatedly denied it. Later, female detectives searched her and found the stolen money in her sock. She was ordered to be detained in the women's prison. Yesterday morning, she was brought to the First Special District District Court. Police Lawyer Wang Yaotang filed a complaint under Article 355, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. Lou Heqing testified to the situation of the defendant snatching the legal tender. Questioned, Wang Fengying confessed that she knew Lou because she was good at dancing. Lou had previously given her two yuan and asked her to dance with him. She was taken to a inn and taken advantage of. The day before yesterday afternoon, Lou gave her another five yuan and asked her to go out with him. Because her clothes had no pockets, she placed the money in her sock. But because she was wary of the past, she was unwilling to go with him, and Lou accused her of snatching the money. Lou, hearing this testimony, admitted that he had invited Wang out for refreshments. Judge Feng questioned them and found Wang Fengying guilty of theft, sentencing her to 30 days of detention, but suspended the sentence for two years in consideration of her first offense.
