Qiu Jiang Wharf Robbery Case Develops; Five More Suspects Apprehended, Tobacco and Soil Boxes Recovered; Involves Deputy Leader of Zhoupu Township and a Deputy Boat Owner

On the evening of June 27th of this year, near midnight, a lighter belonging to the Yongtaihe Tobacco Company, loaded with 39 boxes of cigarettes of various brands, including Golden Mouse, Mao Ling, Little Fairy, Red Seal, Golden, Pin Hai, Old Knife, and Red Tin, was robbed of 37 boxes worth $6,060 at the Qiu Jiang Wharf. The robbers escaped without a trace. The company offered a reward for their capture. Half a month later, customs patrol officers arrested four suspects, Sheng Da, Shi Lang Yin Lang, Gu Er Lang, all from Chongming, and Wang Zhang, the wife of the fugitive Wang Jinsheng, behind the labor camp in Pudong, in a thatched hut. They confessed that the stolen goods were hidden in Zhoupu, Nanhui County, Pudong. More than ten detectives were dispatched to the countryside to pursue the matter. They discovered that the case involved Wu Jiasheng, deputy leader of the Xiukang Township Defense Corps in the fifth district of the county, and Pan Xukui, deputy leader of the Xiunan Township in the third district and leader of the first pai of the seventh jia of the county Defense Corps (previously misreported as the bao chief of the sixth bao of Xiukang Township). They then joined forces with the chief of the first resident office of the county Public Security Bureau and Zhoupu Defense Corps officials to conduct a thorough search and arrest. They arrested Zhang Cailin, Shen Jialu, Wu Jiasheng, and three other suspects. Approximately 27 boxes of cigarettes were found in the ancestral graveyard east of Pan's house. The entire Pan Xukui family had fled without a trace. The case caused a sensation throughout the county and became a common topic of discussion. The water patrol police handed over the three suspects, along with the three men and one woman arrested earlier, to the local court for trial. The recovered stolen goods were returned to the Yongtaihe Company for identification. More than a month later, the water patrol police received another tip that the fugitives were hiding. On the previous day, they arrested Yang Rongsheng (aged 35, from Jiangbei, also known as Da Zaozi) at the intersection of Han Bi Li Road and You Heng Road in the Public Concession. Yang confessed the whereabouts of his accomplices. They then went to No. 36 Hua Ji Road and arrested Xu Fengzao (aged 36, from Haizhou, also known as Xu Gu). Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special Court, where Judge Chui opened the trial. Because the Public Concession police had determined that Yang Rongsheng was involved in the Yulin Road robbery case, he was ordered to be detained pending further investigation on September 2nd. Xu Fengzao was ordered to be handed over to the water patrol police for questioning. Xu confessed that after the stolen goods were transported to Wang Baoming's house in Zhoupu, they hired Zhang Xiaodi's No. 29690 pier boat to transport five boxes to the Nanchang Tobacco Shop in Dayuan, where they were sold. Subsequently, Wang Baoming, Wu Jiasheng, Kang Zhijun, and others hired Wu Sanhe's No. 6832 pier boat to transport the remaining stolen goods to Pan Xukui's house for storage. Upon obtaining this information, the patrol police chief sent detectives to Dongjiadu in the South City and impounded the two boats used to transport the stolen goods pending further investigation. Because ten boxes of cigarettes were still missing and important suspects such as Pan Xukui and Wang Baoming were still at large, they ordered a strict search to bring them to justice.

Supervisor of Sincere Shanghai Branch Huang Huannan Passed Away Yesterday

Huang Huannan, supervisor of the Sincere Shanghai branch, was from Zhongshan, Guangdong Province, and 80 years old. Sixty years ago, he went to Sydney, Australia, to study. Later, he founded the Guang Sheng He Department Store in Keene Street, pioneering the department store business. In 1913, he returned to China. At that time, prominent overseas Chinese businessmen Ma Yingbiao, Ma Yongcan, Zheng Gansheng, and Cai Xing were establishing the Sincere Company in Hong Kong. Huang was hired as the manager of the Guangdong branch of the company. In 1916, he was sent to Shanghai as the manager of the Shanghai branch, and later promoted to his current position. He also served as a director of the Shanghai Commercial Bank, Xinhua Foreign Company, Sincere Life Insurance, and the Guangdong Fellow Townsmen Association in Shanghai. Although he was very old, he was still vigorous and went to the company to manage affairs every day. He was also very friendly and approachable. He had only occasionally felt unwell and rested at home. Recently, his condition worsened and he passed away. The funeral is scheduled for 9:00 PM today at his residence on Laobazi Road, with the burial on the afternoon of the 27th at 1:00 PM. Sanbei and Pinghan Railway Negotiating Water-Land Intermodal Transport; If Progress Smoothly, It Can Be Implemented Within the Year

Domestic intermodal transport has been developing rapidly in recent years and has achieved considerable results, providing convenience for transportation and increasing profits. Last year, the Ministry of Communications and the Ministry of Railways jointly convened shipowners to discuss intermodal transport methods. State-owned shipping companies, such as China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, have successively launched programs, and the progress has been smooth. To adapt to the environment and facilitate freight transport in order to revive the endangered shipping industry, private shipping companies in Shanghai are negotiating intermodal transport with the Pinghan Railway. Sanbei Steamship Company has also sent representatives to negotiate several times. Both parties have expressed their sincerity. However, there is no concrete plan yet. Until recently, there was some initial progress. The matter is being actively prepared. If the progress is smooth, the private Sanbei Company and the Pinghan Railway's water-land intermodal transport can be implemented first this year. Afterwards, larger private shipping companies can continue to participate in the intermodal transport business.

Those who pre-order directly from the magazine before September 5th will enjoy a 30% discount.

Letters

To the Editor: According to Mr. Xi Shiying, the person concerned, the "Shen Bao" newspaper published a news item on the 21st of this month in the "Local News" section, entitled "Content of the Case of Li Shu Company's Embezzlement," which is a new opening. It not only reverses the facts but also damages Shiying's reputation. Yan Gong, the accountant of the Lida Company, embezzled more than 5,000 yuan from the company's accounts and fled to Hangzhou. The company reported the case to the Chengdu Road Police Station, which sent officers to arrest the suspect in Hangzhou and bring him back to Shanghai. He fully confessed to the embezzlement and was sentenced to six months imprisonment and two years of probation by the Criminal Court of the First Special District Court on the 5th of this month. After that, Yan Gong came forward to request permission to publish an advertisement in the newspaper, saying that there was a slight misunderstanding with the company, which led to the lawsuit, in order to reduce the difficulty in finding another job. At that time, the company did not agree to the request because it was far from the truth. Now, the news in the "Shen Bao" states that the company's accountant was accused of embezzlement and that there is obviously another background, which is all based on one-sided facts and is purely speculation. As for all the accounts when the company was reorganized, they have been checked by the old shareholders and there is no fraud, which damages Shiying's reputation. Therefore, we specially request the "Shen Bao" newspaper to correct this. According to this, we hereby request that you make a thorough correction. To the "Shen Bao" newspaper, Lawyer Dang Wanghou, August 24th.

To the Editor: Our association held a solicitation meeting yesterday, with Mr. Chu Fuxin as the temporary chairman. Your newspaper mistakenly wrote Xie Shuren, which should be corrected. To the "Shen Bao" newspaper, Shanghai Silver Money Industry Amateur Friendship Association Preparatory Office, August 24th.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The sky around Shandong is cloudy, with northeasterly to southeasterly winds. The upper and middle reaches of the Yellow River and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River have light and directionless winds. The coast and East China Sea are cloudy with showers and strong northeasterly winds. The climate southeast of the Ryukyu Islands is severe, with cyclones, due to the northwestward movement of the hurricane. The center of the hurricane was within about 60 miles of 22 degrees 20 minutes north latitude and 131 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. The wind force is fierce. Also, the highest temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 86.0 degrees and the lowest was 72.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 95.4 degrees and the lowest was 76.6 degrees.

Sports News

The World Games Open, Every Home Hung Flags and Decorations, Resembling Our Country's New Year Scene - Letter from Li Huitang to this Newspaper

I have been in Berlin for another ten days. (Although the weather here is said to be summer, it is quite similar to the early winter in our country, and the days are short and the nights are long, which is especially strange. The sky dawns at four o'clock in the morning, and the lights are turned on at nine o'clock in the evening.) It is comfortable to live in "Summer Peck Village", and the sleep and food are good, which is gratifying. The conference opened today, presided over by the German head of state "Hitler", with more than 100,000 spectators, an unprecedented grand occasion. The whole city of Berlin is in "Summer Peck Heat", with every home hanging flags and decorations like the New Year scene in our country. Our team entered the arena in order, with Hui as the flag bearer. The flag was large and the pole was heavy, and it took almost three hours. After the event, both hands were sore, which was unbearable. However, it is also sweet to work hard for the country. The transmission of the torch of the conference is especially interesting. The torch was first transmitted from the "Summer Peck" city of Greece (starting on July 20). From that place to Berlin, it is more than 3,000 kilometers. The transmitters walked one kilometer with a torch. The whole journey took more than ten days, with more than 3,000 people. And the last one to arrive at the end of the conference venue was also at the fourth act (evening of August 1st).

Italian Players are Rude, Brutal, and Wild

The conference started with competitions. In the past two days, our country's athletes (track and field) have all failed and did not even qualify for the preliminary round. The distance from the world level can be said to be far away. The Central News Agency has already sent special telegrams about the situation. Our team went to watch the football match between Italy and the United States today. The Italian team's skills were excellent, the performance was pure and skilled, the energy was sufficient, and the running was agile. Unfortunately, they acted on impulse, and they were brutal, wild, and unprecedented. Therefore, although the result was a victory (1 to 0), it was also despised by the audience. Taking advantage of the moment, the reputation will stink forever (the left back was expelled from the arena), which is not advisable. The United States also played quite well, but the shooting skills were not very good, and they could not reverse the defeat, which is a pity. Their fighting spirit was excellent and won the sympathy of the audience. Defeat is not a disgrace. (Norway beat Turkey 3-1 on the same day) (evening of August 3rd).

Germany's Football Achievement is Very Profound

The track and field competition continued today. The representatives of our country bid farewell one after another (we jokingly call the losers graduation). In the afternoon, we went to watch the football match between Germany and Luxembourg. As a result, Germany won a big victory with 9 to 0 (?). The German team's transcendence of football skills is even better than Italy. It is enough to make us open our eyes and guard the forest. The rapid advancement and the infinite changes in strategy and the orderly position are all enough for us to learn from. Moreover, each football skill has reached the top level, and the outstanding performance of the header is especially remarkable. It is heard that Germany has the guidance of famous British teachers and has more practice. The speed of its progress and the excellence of its cooperation are not without reason. Our country's football has been stagnant for the past 20 years. It is imperative to hire elite coaches and trainers, but I don't know if the authorities can thoroughly plan it. On the individual side of the Luxembourg team, there are also good players, but the lack of understanding and a mess, there is no fixed strategy. The importance of cooperation in football can be seen from this.

Sweden Deceived the Enemy and Lost to Japan

Also, Japan won over Sweden by 3 to 1 on the same day, creating an unprecedented upset. Afterwards, it was heard that Sweden deceived the enemy. The Japanese fighting spirit was excellent. In the first half, they lost by two to zero, but they reversed the defeat in the second half, which shows that arrogance will lead to defeat, and the victory or defeat of football is not only based on the superiority or inferiority of football skills, which is even more believed. (Evening of August 4th) Our team will play against England on the 6th, and the loss may be unavoidable. However, you have been working hard these days, and I am confident that there will be a good performance. More details later. Tang Hui, morning of August 5th.

America, Japan, and France Triangular Track and Field Competition, America First, Japan Second

Havas, Paris, 22nd: The track and field teams of the United States and Japan held a triangular competition with the French track and field athletes here today. More than 12,000 spectators watched, and it was very grand. As a result, the United States had the best results, with 131 and a half points, followed by Japan, with 82 and a half points, and then France, with 82 points. Australia Proposes to Launch the Women's Davis Cup, the British Lawn Tennis Association Does Not Express Approval and Points Out Various Difficulties and Questions

(London Reuters) The Australian Lawn Tennis Association has proposed to launch a World Women's Tennis Championship, completely imitating the Davis Cup method. Brooks, the president of the Australian Lawn Tennis Association and former Wimbledon champion, is willing to donate this silver cup. However, according to Poli, the president of the British Lawn Tennis Association, Britain cannot fully support this plan. It is not easy to succeed from a sports or commercial point of view. The public is not as interested in women as they are in men. Therefore, the funding is also a question. Some female tennis players travel abroad for more than six months and are always reluctant to go again. Poli also pointed out a fact that when the British women's team went to France to compete two years ago, there were very few spectators.

European Tour of the World Games Football Team

- Written and Sent by Li Huitang

Arrive in Calcutta

Our team left Yangon on the British mail ship "Aronda" on the morning of June 30th. The journey day and night made the long-distance sailors in the team feel unhappy. They spent the whole journey with short berths as companions. In this "hurricane season," this route is a bit scary, but it is cheaper for the shipping company, saving a lot of food. On the morning of July 2nd, leaning on the railing and looking down, the sea gradually turned yellow. Asking the people in the boat, they said that it was near the mouth of the "Mirror" River in India. The boat was sailing smoothly, without any shaking. Those who were seasick were also suddenly excited and scrambled into the dining room. At 8:30 AM, we entered the river. The forests and fields on both sides were endless. It is heard that it takes another 60 or 70 nautical miles to reach Calcutta by following this river. Just after lunch, Calcutta was far away in sight. Hundreds of people were waiting on the shore to welcome us, including Chen Liang, a leading overseas Chinese businessman, and the president and staff of the Indian Football Association. They boarded the ship and shook hands with us warmly, asking questions one after another. The enthusiasm was touching. After landing, we took a car around the city for a week before rushing to the "Dahua Hotel" to stay. Calcutta is not only the largest city in India, but also in the Far East. Its vast area and dense population are also second to none. In a moment's impression, although not much was seen, the most profound thing is that there are also three "not smalls" here: not few people, not few cars, and not few cattle. Sometimes the pedestrians on the street are really shoulder to shoulder. There are more than 70,000 vehicles in the city. The bustling downtown area often suffers from traffic congestion. The most surprising thing is that you can often see one or two cows on the main roads, bustling places, and in front of large stores, wandering around, unrestrained. Even if they are blocking traffic, the police and pedestrians do not interfere and let them walk freely. It is said that the Buddhists here do not eat beef and worship it as a god. There are releases every year, so there are traces of cattle everywhere in the city. This can also be regarded as a novel sight.

(July 2nd) Nothing happened in the morning. After lunch, the local overseas Chinese community jointly held a tea party to welcome us, and invited European and Indian people to accompany us. During the meeting, everyone gave speeches, all stating the close relationship between the history, classics, and culture of the two ancient countries of China and India. Finally, Dr. Rong thanked us for our gratitude. At 5:30 PM, we went to watch the Class A cycle match here. This match is related to this year's championship, so it is unparalleled. Before our car arrived at the venue, we could see tens of thousands of people moving around from afar. The stands in the arena were made of wood (because the venue is a military venue, permanent buildings are not allowed), and could not accommodate many spectators. Even if it was crowded, it could only accommodate about 20,000 people. However, the enthusiasm for football here is well-known in the Far East. The spectators on the slopes outside the arena are probably 70,000 or 80,000, people like ants, and like stacked Arhats. The salt situation during the football final of the 6th National Games is still not comparable. Since our team's tour to the south, the spectators in all the places we have visited have broken local records, but the excitement today is unprecedented, which is enough to make us open our tongues and stare at our eyes. What is especially new is that the spectators outside the arena who are in the back row and cannot see the whole picture are all holding wooden frames with small mirrors placed on top, and a mirror is suspended below, slightly inclined upwards. The scene of the competition in the arena is reflected and fully visible on the lower mirror. The mirror holders sit cross-legged, watching the movie on the screen, leisurely and happily, without competing with others. This little gadget is also a new experience. Here, there are often football matches, because the weather is too hot, only 50 minutes (5 and a half minutes less). Indian players mostly fight barefoot, and their agility is like a deer running, which benefits a lot. However, sometimes when they encounter those wearing boots, they also suffer a bit. There are no two advantages in the world, which is even more believed here. The football skills here are mostly at a very high level. Short and long passes are all quite accurate, especially short passes are excellent. However, the shooting skills are still lacking, and the header is not very good. In short, what I observed today is that Indian football is still quite pleasing. Although I can't see any particularly outstanding people, everyone is above average. Our team will meet their elite tomorrow, which is not optimistic.

China-India War

(July 4th) Today is the date of the China-India International Competition. This international contact is actually very important. It is heard that the admission tickets were sold out ten days ago. Speculators have doubled or tripled the value of the tickets for sale, which shows that this game is very attractive. The weather was clear and the sun was high on this day. After lunch, from our hostel, we could see the spectators rushing to the arena in a continuous stream. It was said that there were still five or six hours before the start of the game, and the fans did not care about the hard work because of the superiority of the location, and waited under the hot sun with umbrellas. This is a true first-class fan. At 5:30 PM, our team drove into the arena. The spectators were all over the field, and those who could not get in were countless. The lively situation has set an unprecedented record. After the music was played, our team took the following 11 players and took to the field to fight. The first half was 1 to 0, and the result was 1 to 1. The scorer was Jinshun.

Bao Jiaping

Li Tiansheng Mai Shaohan

Chen Zhenhe Xu Yahui Liang Rongzhao

Zheng Jiliang Tan Jiangbai Li Huitang Sun Jinshun Yang Shuiyi

After a little leg training, they lined up in front of the stand and shook hands and saluted a certain Indian prince, the president of the Football Association. After the ceremony, the game started. 19 of the opponents were barefoot, which took advantage of the dry and hard field today. Since we started playing football, we have never encountered opponents who played barefoot. Today, we broke the topic and had a special feeling after contacting them, which was strange and interesting and indescribable. They were good at managing the ball, and the passing and passing were excellent. Xu Yahui in our team had just recovered from illness and had not played for half a month. Today, he took to the field again, but his strength was poor. Rongzhao's position was also poor, and the middle and right sides were repeatedly invaded by the enemy. The performance of the forwards, Jiliang and Jiangbai, was the most abnormal. Jiangbai could not use his header skills, which affected the whole line. In the first half, Jinshun scored a goal and took the lead by one to zero. In the second half, the Indian team's offensive became more intense, and our team was surrounded and in danger many times. Fortunately, they lacked shooting skills and did not lose. Before the end of the game, Shaohan was penalized 12 yards for stealing the ball, so he was tied at 1 to 1. After the game, all parties commented that this free kick was inappropriate. In short, our team did not make any amazing revelations in today's game. The whole team, except for Jiaping, Tiansheng, Zhenhe, and Huitang, who could maintain the usual bear, the rest were far inferior to the measures taken in Yangon the week before. Was it because there were too many spectators and they were afraid of the arena? Was it related to the hot weather?

The Chinese football team lost to the British team by zero to two.

Diligent Bookstore Publication: World Sports Pictorial. Excellent Value, Enthusiastic Pre-Orders.

All Sectors of the City's Party, Government, Business, and Academic Communities Prepare to Commemorate Confucius' Birthday. A Commemoration Ceremony will be held on the 28th in the Dacheng Hall of the People's Education Center.

The 28th of this month is the National Day of the First Teacher Confucius' Birthday. Various party, government, business, academic, agricultural, labor, and military institutions in the city, including the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Education Association, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, the Municipal Farmers' Association, and the Garrison Headquarters, have already begun preparations. It has been decided that a joint commemoration ceremony for the birthday of the First Teacher Confucius will be held at 10:00 am on the morning of that day in the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road in the Nanshi. The presidium has nominated seven people to serve as chairpersons: Mayor Wu, Tong Xingbai, Yang Hu, Wang Xiaoxiang, Huang Zaoxiong, Yu Zhenhui, and Lu Jingshi. The Municipal People's Education Center has already begun preparations. The ritual vessels for worshipping Confucius originally displayed in the Dacheng Hall will soon be moved to the lecture hall for public viewing. The Municipal Education and Social Affairs Bureaus will also issue a notice to all large, medium, and small schools and factories in the city to take a day off on that day and celebrate with flag-raising. In addition to holding commemoration ceremonies and reporting on Confucius's actions of diligent practice and love of learning within the schools, each school will also send one representative to participate in the general assembly.

Education Commissioner's Itinerary for Inspecting the Northwest

In order to subsidize the expenses of middle and elementary schools in Gansu, Suiyuan, Ningxia, and Qinghai provinces and help their educational development, the Board of Directors for the Management of the British Boxer Indemnity Fund has specifically appointed Mr. Derek Rowntree, a British director (Mr. Rowntree is an economic expert and professor at Yenching University, has been in China for many years, and usually pays special attention to rural handicrafts in China), and requested the Ministry of Education to appoint Commissioner Guo Youshou to inspect the actual needs of each province for reference. After Mr. Rowntree and Mr. Guo met in Beiping, they, along with Mr. Mei Yiqi, Dean of Studies at Yenching University, left Beiping on the 20th and arrived in Guisui on the 21st. The planned itinerary is to stay one week each in Suiyuan, Ningxia, and Qinghai provinces and two weeks in Gansu province. After the inspection is completed, Commissioner Guo Youshou will be ordered by the Ministry of Education to go to Shaanxi to inspect the National Northwest College of Agriculture and Forestry. This trip will take six weeks and is expected to return to Nanjing at the end of September or the beginning of October.

The fourth group of students going to the United States in this session, including Yang Qin, Wang Liwo, Chen Shicai, Zhou Jianru, Zhang Shaochu, Di Fuyu, Qiu Shengyuan, Chen Chan, Yu Weizhong, Wei Sun, Huai Ci, Xu Zhong and 92 others, departed yesterday afternoon on the Japan Empress, the largest passenger ship of the Pacific Mail Steamship Company. News of the Organization of the Education and Film Industries: The Electrical Education Supplies Company Holds its Inaugural Meeting at the Education Film Association. Fang Zhi, Pan Gongzhan, and Others Serve as Directors.

In recent years, the Ministry of Education has spared no effort in promoting film and broadcasting education. This city, as a pioneer in promoting electrical education, recognizes that the reliance on foreigners for electrical education supplies hinders the progress of electrical education. Prominent figures in the city's education circles, such as Pan Gongzhan, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Gongsu, Chen Hezhen, and Hu Shuyi, as well as the backbone members of the four major film companies in the city, namely Mingxing, Lianhua, Yihua, and Xinhua, have jointly initiated the organization of a China Film Education Supplies Company. Preparations have been underway for almost a year, and the share capital has now been fully raised. In accordance with the law, the inaugural meeting was held yesterday at the premises of the China Education Film Association. More than 20 shareholders attended, and Wang Baoyun was sent by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to attend. The meeting started at 3:00 pm. The company's articles of association were approved, the share capital was examined, and Fang Zhi, Pan Gongzhan, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Gongsu, Zhou Bangjun, Sun Daosheng, Tao Shengbai, Bian Yuying, and Lu Shibai were elected as directors. Zhang Shankun and Tong Xingbai were elected as alternate directors, and Yang Minshi and Zhao He were elected as supervisors, and Yan Chuntang and Wu Bangfan were elected as alternate supervisors. The company's business scope includes (1) producing, distributing, and reprinting domestic and foreign educational films, and (2) manufacturing and managing projectors and other audio-visual educational supplies. All kinds of film and sound projectors, amplifiers, generators, transformers, and other application objects are available for distribution. In addition, small film projectors, film copying machines, and film processing machines are being ordered from abroad. The company is currently looking for a factory site and business department property and will officially open as soon as the arrangements are completed. The mailing address remains temporarily at the original address of the preparatory office at No. 86, Lane 273, Jiaozhou Road.

Minzhi School Opens Today

The Minzhi Middle School on Weihaiwei Road will hold its opening ceremony at 8:00 am today, and elementary school classes will also start at the same time. A notice has already been published in newspapers informing new and old students, both male and female, from both local and out-of-town locations to complete enrollment and class attendance procedures as soon as possible or apply for leave to avoid truancy and to facilitate the reservation of places. There are still some places available in the elementary school, except for Spring Grade 3. Middle school, except for Autumn Grade 3, which is full, will hold another enrollment on the 30th. Boarding is available for both boys and girls, with separate facilities and management. This year's school buildings have been expanded, and in addition to most of the old teachers, more than ten new teachers have been hired, including Wu Huixuan from Datong, Ma Chongzong from Meiji, Huang Yuqing from South China, Yang Rencai from Daxia, and Cai Chanzhen from the Shanghai Art College. Finance: A Certain Bank Opens Cash Transactions, Call Money Weakens and then Stabilizes. Closed for Confucius' Birthday on the 27th.

Although the price of pure gold in London fell yesterday, due to the rumor that a certain bank would open cash transactions for 700 bars at a price of 27 yuan, the sellers in the market became enthusiastic, and the result was neither gain nor loss. In the early morning, the overseas silver market saw London rise and the United States remain flat, and the forward silver price in Montreal was unchanged or rose by one basis point. The exchange rate was flat, the price of gold in London fell by one penny, the central bank's bid price was announced, and the prices for both the United States and England were flat. The customs gold unit shrank by two basis points, and the standard call money price fell to 1123 yuan and 90 cents. The over-the-counter preparatory transaction was about 27 yuan and 50 to 80 cents. During this period, Hengyu sold slightly, and Wanxing slightly bought but mostly held. The opening in the morning was slightly lower, and after the opening, the sellers were slightly enthusiastic and continued to fall. Major players bought one after another. Although the HSBC bid prices for England and the United States were flat, due to the rumor that a certain bank would open cash transactions at a price of 27 yuan, the buyers became more enthusiastic, and the silver balance tax was announced to rise by 75. The price gradually rose back, lacking changes midway, and remained stable at noon. In the afternoon, only 20 cents were traded, and the demand was scarce, with no vitality. Securities: The Last Day of August, Market Prices for Public Bonds are Mostly Inverted.

Yesterday, the Chinese Securities Exchange was the last day of futures for August. Because the 27th was Confucius' birthday and the market was closed, the market was stopped one day earlier this month. The market was mostly short covering, and there was very limited long covering. Because there were many swap transactions, the market prices rose and fell without a fixed pattern. Although there have been changes in the environment, the market seemed to be temporarily insensitive to the worries due to the chip relationship. Today, only one month of futures for September is traded. Based on the environmental speculation, there should be a slight rebound. The 96 was pulled up several times and finally fell. The opening sentiment yesterday was relatively weak, and the market prices were close to strong and far to weak, and most of them were inverted. In particular, the B bond was inverted by 1 yuan, which was the largest. The market prices were compared to be small, ranging from 12 cents to 40 cents. The secondary market was still dominated by swap transactions. D bond and B bond had a slight long covering trend. D bond No. 72 had a large number of cash deliveries, and the long positions of B bond were too crowded. The other bonds were still slightly short covering, and the market prices were inverted again and again. The afternoon opening was the most popular, and short covering was still the most important. Market prices were mostly good for 10 cents to 30 cents, and most were still inverted. However, the D bond was small for 20 cents this month, and the closing prices of D and B bonds were long covering, with near-term falling and far-term rising. The rest continued to be good for 10 cents to 40 cents. The market price fluctuated indefinitely when the chips were mutually squeezed, which was not the regularity of the market price. As a result, D bond and B bond were small for 35 cents this month, and the rest uniformly rose from 12 cents to 45 cents. The 96 was small for 25 cents. The total transaction volume was 13,585,000 yuan. The results of the rise and fall are listed on the left for comparison (unit: yuan, transaction unit: 100 yuan).

Cotton Yarn: Short Covering is Done According to the Market. Chen Cotton Almost Stopped Being Auctioned. The Low Price Once Reached 41 Yuan and 20 Cents. As a Result, it Still Fell by 1 Yuan and 85 Cents.

Because the settlement of the cotton market in this month's period is imminent, the long positions are based on the abundant cotton production. The Ningbo Xinyao cotton industry has already been coming in continuously. The general short covering can only be painfully cut according to the market, and the market is showing a tragic decline. When the market opened in the afternoon, the low peak reached 41 yuan and 20 cents, which was 3 yuan and 25 cents lower than the previous day, which reached the limit of the board. After the profit takers made up, it rebounded by 1 yuan and 40 cents, and compared to it, it still fell by 1 yuan and 85 cents.

New Cotton also Enters the 9 Yuan Mark

When the market opened in the morning, the price of American cotton in the Southern set fell by 5 to 7 basis points, and Indian cotton was flat. The price of Osaka Sanpin Cotton rose by 11 cents. The market was quite worried. Because the long positions of Chen Cotton in the August period participated in the abundant new cotton production year, there was absolutely no intention to receive Chen Cotton. As a result, the table was panicked, and there was a trend of a thousand-mile crash. The market fell sharply. Shen Ji and Hengyi vigorously increased their stakes, and Xincheng, Dayan, Yuanxingchang, and Jifeng all made up for short positions. As a result, the August period fell by 2 yuan and 35 cents compared to the closing price of the previous day. The distant months broke the 9 yuan mark and fell by 4.5 to 5.7 cents. When the market opened in the afternoon, this month fell by another 90 cents. However, when the auction reached the near month, profit takers made a large number of offsets and were firm, and the distant months returned to outside the 9 yuan mark. Unexpectedly, the sellers came like a tidal surge at the close, and the price fell sharply by 30 cents. As a result, each month rebounded by 5 cents to 20 cents compared to the morning closing price. Dafeng and Xincheng bought in the morning and Dou Chadu out in the afternoon. Shen Ji bought 6,800 piculs, Changfeng 9,500 piculs, Gengfeng 4,500 piculs, Xingchang 2,400 piculs, Hexing 2,000 piculs, Runkang 2,100 piculs, Juxing 4,600 piculs, Hengyi 3,200 piculs, Tongji 2,400 piculs, Yongyu 4,000 piculs, Deda 2,200 piculs. Spring and Autumn

Cotton Prices Fall Daily, Yarn Market Also Reports Tragic Decline, This Month to $195.60

The yarn market initially fell in the morning, recovered slightly in the afternoon, but ultimately continued to decline. This was mainly because the August contract only has one more business day tomorrow. Many parties, seeing the daily decline in cotton prices and the easing of cotton yarn costs, were unwilling to take delivery. Floating positions were mostly settled based on the new market, and the decline was remarkably strong. The forward contracts were dragged into the whirlpool, with all months breaking through the $200 mark.

Forward Contracts Have Broken Through $200

Standard Yarn Market Opening: Because the August yarn contract only has tomorrow left for trading, most floating positions, seeing the abundant cotton harvest and expecting cotton prices to fall, were unwilling to take delivery of cotton yarn. As a result, the market became increasingly weak, with all months declining in a straight line. At the same time, spot yarn business stagnated, and people were even more discouraged. Market prices fell step by step, with each month breaking through the $200 mark. Dafu, Xuan Yi, and Shen Ji were all actively selling, while Feng Nuli also put out large volumes. Dachang, Xingchang, Senkangde, and Da Linjin were also considerable. As a result, each month fell by $2.40 to $1.60 compared to the previous day's closing price. In the afternoon trading session, the current month remained weak, with bids reaching as far as the distant months. After the trading session, it was said that the Sichuan brokers still had some transactions. Short sellers pushed forward, and the last three months rose back outside the $200 mark. Unexpectedly, all months closed lower, and the decline intensified. As a result, each month rose by $1.40 to $1.60 compared to the morning closing price. Market transactions were frequent. The morning session closed at 1:15, and the afternoon session was extended, opening at 3:00 and closing after 6:00, which shows how enthusiastic speculators must be. According to reports, Dafu bought in the afternoon after selling in the morning, Tongji 3,000 bales, Hengyi 6,200 bales, Juyu 5,150 bales, Shenji 2,450 bales, Renyi 1,150 bales, Dachangcheng 1,250 bales, Changfeng 3,650 bales, Jinghua 1,250 bales, Daji 3,650 bales, and Xiacheng 1,700 bales. Shengji bought in 5,450 bales, Xingchang 3,550 bales, Senkang 1,850 bales, Dachang 3,800 bales, Shengyuan 1,050 bales, and Taichang 1,800 bales. The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed below.

Spot Yarn Also Falls by $1-$2

Spot yarn sales were average. According to a survey, various brokers purchased a total of 927 bales throughout the day, with selling prices falling by $1.20 or more. The purchase amounts for each broker are listed below:

Sichuan: 200 Shantou: 10 Inland: 255

Guangdong: 170 Jiangxi: 20 Changsha: 250

Hankou: 5 Peers: 17

Slight Rise in Third-Grade Yarn

Osaka Telegraph, 24th: Third-grade futures yarn rose by 50 cents to $1.30, with the near month at $209.50 and the distant month at $209. Futures cotton rose by 5 cents to 25 cents, with the near month at $64.70 and the distant month at $62.25.

Grain: Spot Sales Quiet, Bulls Emerge in This Month's Flour, a Significant Drop of More Than 5 Cents

Yesterday's flour market returned to normal. After the opening in the morning, foreign wheat (Chicago) was slightly higher by a small amount for the near month, and better by several points for the distant months. Canadian wheat rose by about 10 cents. There was no foreign guidance to follow. The spot wheat market was already sluggish, and flour sales were also quiet. Moreover, trading for this month is about to end, leaving little room for maneuver. Large and small bulls emerged one after another. New short positions for distant months arose upon hearing the news. Therefore, the market fell step by step from the opening, continuing the downward trend. By the afternoon closing, the domestic factories slightly increased their intake of distant contracts, and the momentum finally stabilized. As a result, compared to the weekend closing, this month fell by 5.25 cents, September and November each fell by a small 4 cents, October fell by a small 3.75 cents, December fell by a small 2.1 cents, and January fell by a small 2.75 cents.

Spot Merchants Rush to Hedge Sell, Futures Wheat Drops Step by Step, October Falls by a Whole Dime

Yesterday's futures wheat market saw spot factories become less enthusiastic, and the depreciation of medium-grade wheat was particularly severe. The delivery period for this month is approaching rapidly. In general, merchants, seeing that the delivered goods from the new harvest are all medium-quality, have become less interested in taking delivery. Therefore, after the opening in the morning, bulls sold off one after another, and spot merchants also began to hedge sell in succession. As a result, the situation in the morning declined step by step, with near and distant months falling by 6 to 9 cents. However, foreign wheat reports were still calm, but the downward trend was already quite weak. In the afternoon, floating short positions covered, and opportunistic traders entered the market, gradually stabilizing the situation. Therefore, the afternoon only fluctuated between 1 and 2 cents, resulting in a situation where the market started with a decline and ended with stabilization. Overall, compared to last Saturday's closing price, August fell by a small 4 cents, October fell by a dime, November fell by a small 9 cents, and September and December each fell by a small 8 cents. Spot wheat, due to sluggish sales at factories, had slightly relaxed receiving standards, and prices were considering tightening slightly. However, hawkers were unwilling to lower prices, so a stalemate temporarily formed. No bales were delivered throughout the day.

New Sesame from Yangzhou Enters the Market, New Soybeans Become Popular Due to Rumors of Japanese Merchants Buying

Yesterday, more than 200 packages of new sesame from Yangzhou arrived. Because the goods were low-grade, the local market selected 71 packages, with a price opening at $9.40. This year's product is significantly inferior to last year's, with a quality of only 834. This is largely due to excessive rainfall, which affected the color. The yield cannot yet be accurately measured, but it is estimated to be about 60-70%. Large batches of new goods from the Jinpu Railway are expected to arrive around the Mid-Autumn Festival. Transactions involving foreign firms dumping new sesame were seen as restrained yesterday. Both buyers and sellers adopted a defensive posture at a price of $13, so no transactions occurred. Due to widespread rumors of Japanese merchants buying in Jiujiang, new soybeans became sought after in the local market. The market's sentiment was disrupted. Oil mills lowered prices to purchase, so the market price suddenly rose by more than 20 cents. More than 2,000 packages of Jiangqiao soybeans were transacted. The local market sold more than 1,400 packages of Changzhou buffalo hide yellow beans and more than 200 packages of Eryang soybeans, as well as Zhuxi soybeans. Chen soybeans were taken by the Jianshe office to the Siping Street bean cake factory. The market price rose by 16-17 cents compared to the previous market.

Rice Market Prices Were Flat and Weak, Customer Xian Rice Had Strong Sales

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, sources from various brokers arrived with a total of ten points and seven numbers, totaling more than 3,000 dan. Customer sales remained poor. Baowei Qingniao Brokers also purchased 400-500 packages. Therefore, the market situation was high, stable, and weak. Except for high-quality goods, the market prices for thick early japonica and thin indica were unaffected. Medium and low qualities all fell by a few points. Duyangjian and Yinbianyuan were both still stable. Dongxin arrived with more than 1,000 dan, but the outflow decreased, and prices fell by a dime.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 34-35 ships arrived from various routes in Hexia. Among the goods on the market, white japonica sales were slightly active, Bianyuan was still good, and the remaining goods were all sluggish. The white japonica market price fell by about a dime. The prices for various indica and thin indica were flat and weak. Bianyuan also showed a soft trend. The price of Dongxin japonica fell by a small dime. The new japonica from Zhuanqiao that opened on the market yesterday was from the Dongxin route. The opening price was slightly higher, which was due to the difference between the good and bad qualities of the Hexia factories.

(Customer Xian) The arrival of Customer Xian rice was very strong yesterday and the day before, especially with more goods arriving from the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. A total of more than 30,000 packages arrived newly in two days, and the number of Hankou arriving in the yarn market accounted for two-thirds. Although customer sales have been strong in recent days, the large number of new rice arrivals has ultimately put downward pressure on market prices, ranging from a few points to a dime. Yesterday, our Customer rice sales were all active. The Beiyang Brokers purchased 2,500 packages of Xiangjing, and the Cantonese Brokers purchased 6,000-7,000 packages of rough rice. The others were all purchased by the local market, with limited purchases by scattered brokers. Because new rice is being launched successively in various places, inland brokers have lacked appetite. A total of 2,000 packages of Jiangxi rice, 3,900 packages of Hunan rice, 600 packages of Wenzhou-Taizhou rice, and more than 8,000 packages of Ying rough rice were offered throughout the day.

Piece Goods and Cotton Cloth: Only Printed Fabrics Remain Stable

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market was affected by the estimated increase in domestic cotton production and the uniform weakness of foreign cotton and standard yarn, and the market trended downward. White goods bore the brunt. Each brand of Japanese factory goods, including fine cloth, fine twill, coarse cloth, coarse twill, market cloth, and 84 gray cloth, all fell in price one after another, falling from 5 cents to a dime per bolt. The sales prices of coarse twill and coarse cloth from local factories remained stable, while fine cloth and fine twill slightly recovered by 5 cents per bolt. However, the demand for printed and plain tribute cloth, serge, satin, and printed flannel from various Chinese and foreign factories remained strong, and the sales prices were stable. Customers from the Northwest Shaanxi Province gradually increased their orders. Although the weather is arid, the impact on cotton production is still minimal. Printed fabrics in Sichuan, Hunan, and Yunnan are also still active, causing all factories' production to fall short of delivery. Guangdong and Guangxi have seen a sharp decline in sales due to the current situation. Brokers from the North, including Tianjin and Jinan, are still purchasing large quantities of line cloth, coarse cloth, printed tribute cloth, and serge. Inland brokers have gradually increased their purchases of light-weight coarse cloth, local factory fine twill, colored line cloth, printed tribute cloth, and serge.

Western Tribute Cloth is Searched for Eagerly

Ordinary Yuanqing tribute cloth has been in great demand from the Changsha and Chongqing brokers, and the stock inside and outside the Shanghai market is severely depleted. Both domestic and foreign goods have risen in price across the board. In particular, Western goods priced at $5.00 are particularly popular. Most merchants have already searched and exhausted their stocks. Because no new goods have been imported, Japanese goods priced at $5.59 must be sold for about $5.00, causing customers to universally need to purchase Western goods. Yesterday, ordinary Yuan tribute cloths from Shunquan, Longtai, Shishi, Shaoshi, and Deji Six Filial Garden and Lihe Naotiangong, etc., priced around $5.00, were all sold out. Their popularity is comparable to Polish woolen cloth. Yesterday, Guohuo Zhanghua Yuan tribute cloth sold for $4.50, Sima Xiangru from Abe, Ichito, and Mitsui sold for $4.95, Anli Jubaopen $7.70, and Gongyi Jinshita $6.60.

Silk and Tea: Overseas Silk Markets Feel Very Depressed

Yesterday, there was no market in the New York silk market. Yokohama spot prices maintained their original prices, and the futures trend was loose and weak. The price of silk in Lyon did not move. The atmosphere in foreign markets was very depressed. Domestic users also lacked vitality. Yesterday, only white-head merchants had some transactions. In addition, transactions with white factories and Shandong brokers were also very quiet.

Ping Shui Bulk Transactions Were Smooth

Yesterday, the green tea market situation was slightly more active. Brokers from England, America, France, and other countries had sales of green tea from various routes. Among them, the bulk category of Pingshui was the most active, with more than 8,600 boxes transacted. The top price was $41.75, which was still considered stable. As for Luzhuang, Tuzhuang, Zhenmei, and Zhucha, the market also improved compared to before. However, the selling price of Zhenmei tended to be soft, and the Zhucha market price was solid. The situation remained inconsistent between firmness and softness.

According to the Tea Merchants Association report, yesterday there were continued sporadic transactions of green tea. Xiehe purchased more than 200 boxes of Zhenmei, estimated at $104 for the four famous brands, and $71 for the Tunzhen brand. Baolong purchased more than 200 boxes of Huizhen, priced at $58 to $60. Fushi and Hua tea each purchased more than 100 boxes, priced at $60 to $70. Yongxing also purchased a small amount of each. Xiehe also purchased another 600 boxes of Xiaozhenmei, priced at $25 to $28. In addition, since the founding of the Xiezhuhui Yuan Tea Market, there have been one or two transactions of Gongxi. Yesterday, there were 32 more boxes, with a transaction price of $100. Tongfu purchased more than 400 boxes of Pingshui another colored Zhucha, priced at $57. Bulk transactions were relatively quiet.

Sugar Market: Futures Dongbai Prices Loosened - Reaching a Total of Weakly 50,000 Packages in Recent Days

Yesterday, the sugar market weakened as the underground trading of Dongbai futures in recent days offered more than 40,000 packages at lower prices. Yesterday, the Lifang factory continued to offer 4,000 packages, estimated at (J) $6.15, (N) $5.95, and SH $5.75. Therefore, the Public Association's market assessment was also weak. Second and fourth grade rough white sugar was transacted at $6.65. Dongbai No. 4 was transacted at $21.30, re-exported at $6.30, and No. 8 spot was transacted at $21.13, re-exported at $6.10, all down by a small amount. No. 9 called for the original price. Yesterday, the Jinxin Dahua local factory's Mianbai No. 1 goods were transported to Lianyungang by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Taishun wheel with more than 2,000 packages. In addition, there were several hundred packages of Hainan red. A broker on the Foreign Firm Street offered more than 1,000 packages of Hainan red, priced at $12.50 to $12.60, which were then purchased in full by the Tianjin brokers. Although the price fell back, the market trend was still popular. In addition, the Chaozhou brokers offered more than 80 packages of Qingshi red, priced at $15.40, which was slightly looser than before. 17,500 packages of Dutch rough white sugar were transported by the Zhi Geni Canada wheel yesterday.

The joint venture company held its first tender for Cantonese rough white sugar of the week yesterday, with a total quota of more than 6,000 packages. The tender price was as before. The Shunde factory's Wuyang white was sold for 395 packages at $21.60, the Shixin factory sold another 140 packages at $21.40, and the Shizhong white sand sold 20 packages at $19.30, for a total of 555 packages transacted.

Dried Fruits and Nuts: Lanzhu Branch Prices Tighten, Hainan Longan Arrives in Large Quantities, Price Falls

Hainan Longan: Yesterday, two ships arrived from Sichuan and Shandong, and the arrival of goods gradually increased. In addition, the price of Guangzhou Longan has been falling for days, and sentiment is trending downward. The market price has become depressed. Goods previously priced at $5.30 were offered yesterday, falling by a dime, breaking through the $50 mark. Therefore, it is expected that today's market offering will be difficult to improve.

Lanzhu Branch: Recently, due to the lack of arrival and inventory, the market offering has tightened, reaching $30, which is a dime higher than the first market. It is said that Taiyuan was originally scheduled to arrive yesterday, but it has not arrived by evening. It is likely that the delay was caused by a storm en route. It is said that the number of arrivals this time will definitely increase, and the owners' intentions are quite high, and they have sent telegrams requesting an increase in price, demanding to hold at $35.

Hardware: Dongbai Iron is Dumped in Sichuan

Since the establishment of the Zhongshan and Asia factories (Japanese companies) in the local area for Dongbai iron, the output has reached about 10,000 sheets per day. The local factory's construction brokers' sales market only sells about 4,000 sheets per day. Therefore, the agents and distributors have tried their best to promote it to the inland rivers and the Yangtze River, but the average daily sales volume is only 3,000 sheets. It is passed that Japanese businessmen are paying attention to the Sichuan brokers' business, so the market price for Sichuan brokers' sales is also particularly low, by about 2 cents per sheet. Therefore, large amounts of sales are being shipped to Sichuan every day, with 7,000-8,000 sheets being shipped. The market price is about $1 per seven-foot sheet, and about 81-82 cents per six-foot sheet. The agents and distributors can deduct a commission of 2-3 cents per sheet. Therefore, the sales of British-Bidd and other goods have been greatly affected.

Women and Night

— Zhou Xian

Women and night seem to be inseparable. A night without women to embellish it is lonely and chilling. And women who are not active at night also seem unable to express the mystery of women.

Naturally, in the early morning, in the daytime, there are also many women active in our society. But those women are either female workers, women... There are also various other women who exchange labor for life. But when the night falls, covering the earth, the wails of life are covered by an atmosphere of joy. In the realm of night, all there is are women and laughter, or laughing women.

The bowstring vibrates on the erhu string. Sharp and clear voices, accompanied by the erhu sound, come from large restaurants, large hotels, and so-called residences that look like mansions. Then, there is a burst of hearty laughter. Awkwardly, it is the laughter of men. Sharply, it is the laughter of women. Under the ghostly lights, in the splendid melodies, laughing men, embracing laughing women, stepping at a light pace, are so leisurely. In the playground, men are constantly winking at women, and women are also constantly flirting with men. There, all women are so mysterious. In massage parlors, there are even more young and beautiful girls. There are also women who perform obscene and immoral acts, doing incredible work to win the laughter of men. The most common are naturally the goddesses standing on the street. Under the dim lights, they radiate a mysterious allure with unnatural smiles.

Why do women have to be active at night? I think, perhaps they can hide under the lights, hidden under the powder and rouge, the traces of the lashings of life? But our night, in reality, is fortunately filled with women, which is why it is so mysterious. Otherwise, our society would really be too lonely!

Night at the Jai Alai Court

— Fang Zheng

Multicoloured neon lights illuminate a horizontal English sign reading "auditorium". The entrances and exits are crowded with gentlemanly tycoons, well-dressed young men, strangely dressed and flamboyantly attired young ladies, slick-haired hooligans... The Indian doorman keeps shouting, "Pass! Pass!" Then a large group of people are swallowed in, and then another large group of people are spat out.

The magnificent architecture, the bright electric lights, make people forget the night. Luxury, extravagance, the lights seem to be a place of production, but also a place to wear away national aspirations. However, in order to satisfy certain desires, people ignore their own survival and flock to it in droves!

After the people are seated, several players walk into the large wire mesh cage, wearing red, yellow, and green sports uniforms. First, a man in a suit blows a whistle, which is considered a simple opening ceremony, and the players begin the game. A wooden ball, like a duck egg, jumps back and forth, strangely orderly. One can't help but admire the superb sporting techniques of the Europeans and Americans! After one round is completed, the number cards under the players' surnames hanging high up change with the victories and defeats. Then the audience begins to stir. The banknotes at the ticket office fly like butterflies. Two dollars, five dollars, ten dollars, twenty dollars, thirty dollars... People seem to have gone mad, forgetting the money earned with blood and sweat, forgetting everything, even forgetting themselves.

"Hiss... hiss... hiss..." A command announces the end of one game. People's hearts are beating anxiously, but when they realize their disappointment, they are extremely resentful. There are also those who are laughing and happy, but they are ultimately in the minority!

Soon the second game begins, and the audience goes even crazier! Because "failure is the mother of success". They firmly believe in this famous saying! Listen to the sound of madness!

"Hey! Come on, one Caleja, two Chremadi!"

"Come on, two Bilbaos, two Yisgaos!"

But the result is Yahampei. They keep repeating this, muttering "bad luck", going on and on, twelve o'clock, one o'clock... But their spirit is even more invigorated and interested than when they are working. If there were no clock in the world, I believe they would definitely think that there is no distinction between day and night.

According to someone familiar with this way of life, the income here every night is at least around five or six thousand dollars, and half of it is contributed by our Chinese people. Although some people say: "China is extremely poor."

Night at the Confucian Temple Park

— Yao Mingran

When the scorching sun has collected its flames, and the night breeze is sending coolness: it is the Confucian Temple at night, the most lively moment. The stream-like crowds flow, making the usually quiet Confucian Temple Road as bustling as Nanjing Road!

The guard at the gate cannot control this large force of people. Entering the gate, you feel the heat rising, looking around, all are filled with black crowds, some sitting, some standing, some dozing off! Some chatting and talking! Dachengmen is the key fortress of cool breeze, attracting crowds who are greedy for coolness, like plainclothes teams, taking encircling skirmish lines to consolidate their positions!

Pushing through the crowd like a scout, it is finally difficult to reach the front of the steps of the Dacheng Hall. Although there are a few swaying trees trying to drive away the hot air for us, how can they resist it completely? There, tea shopkeepers, the bourgeoisie, and the proletariat surround the steps, just like a screen!

The road is getting harder and harder to walk! Sneakily and slowly walking to the city library side, the wild lotus leaves in the pond in front of the library are quietly standing tall and graceful. A few clear calls of the gold-threaded frogs are enough for the crowd suffocated by the hot gods to breathe! Because of the clear and melodious sound, it also attracts a lot of crowds. In the middle, one person suffering from Hysteria-like disease raised his head and laughed, attracting sidelong glances from others. Dozens of gazes focused on his face, scanning him until he was embarrassed and turned to sneak away! Further down, it is the business department of Guanshengyuan. The brilliant lights illuminate the entire room, and the rotating electric fans are busy non-stop. The moon hangs high, the bright and clean stars, bathing in the river, reflecting snowy silver light. At the same time, the fireflies on the water's edge, flashing and sparkling, embellish the Confucian Temple on a summer night!

It is nine o'clock, and the bell urging you to return home is loudly warning you, saying goodbye to the Confucian Temple at night. The fluorescent lights and the sound of frogs are swirling in my mind, becoming my spiritual companions on my way home.

Night at Bansong Garden

— Ying Dai

The Bansong Garden at the South Railway Station, in the recent three years, has been opening its night garden every summer. This year's night garden has already opened. In addition to the usual various embellishments, Ding Wan'e has been specially invited to sing Shanghai opera in the Four Sides Hall. Open-air movies are shown in the open space. On Wednesdays, Saturdays, and Sundays, there are also fireworks displays.

It was a Saturday night. Out of curiosity, I went to Bansong Garden to experience the night scenery of this garden. When I arrived at Niusong Garden, it was about seven o'clock in the evening. Yunfei cars and Xiangsheng cars carried park visitors one after another and dropped them off at the entrance of Bansong Garden. Inside Bansong Garden, the lights were all lit up at this time, turning into a night scene.

As I walked into the garden, passing through the winding mud road, I saw electric lights installed everywhere among the green trees, reflecting a kind of green light, making the garden feel even more secluded. Those summer cicadas hiding under the leaves, thinking that the lights were sunlight, mistakenly recognizing night as day, were happily singing in the wind again.

Temporarily pleased, I climbed to the highest earthen mound and sat in the thatched pavilion. Looking around, it was all dark, I could see nothing, only occasionally could I catch a glimpse of a star or two of light through the branches. A cool breeze blew in gusts, landing on my body, making me feel cool all over, forgetting the scorching heat I felt when I sat at home during the day.

Inside the pond, I remember that last year there was a Three Pools Mirroring the Moon protruding in front of the lake heart pavilion, but this year, opposite the lake heart pavilion, a Jiaxing misty rain building was built. Electric lights along the lake were reflected in the water, which would immediately make you think of the night scenery on the shore of West Lake. Rowboats floated gently on the water, and the tourists sang songs in the darkness when they were happy.

Here, loving men and women whispered sweet nothings in the winding paths, and noble gentlemen led their wives, children, and daughters-in-law to leisurely tour the night garden. Male and female workers also came to this garden to breathe and recover from the fatigue of their daytime work. There were indeed many visitors in the garden!

It is said that the fireworks will not be set off until 11:30. I circled around the garden alone several times and really could not wait. I had no choice but to sacrifice not watching them. When I walked out, I found the game of Wenhu in Jiangshang Caotang, and the lotus flowers in the lotus pond had bloomed. A pool of lotus leaves was so fat that it was hard to see. After leaving the park gate, I went back the same way.

Changing Nests and Mating Birds

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Five: Brocade Happiness Repeated, Sounds Resonate on Emerald Leaves; Bridal Gown Startlingly Tried On, Tears Wet the Silk Gauze

He walked to the washstand, reaching into the basin to wash his face, only to realize he was still holding the teacup. So, he put down the teacup and laughed heartily to himself. Aunt Liu hurried into the room, asking what was the matter. He had already hastily washed up, not even drinking his tea, and tucked away the letter and painting, hurrying out. Originally, he hoped to see Menglan on the road, thank her, and perhaps have a chance to speak with her. But his plan was misguided. On this day, Menglan felt the impending doom, disheartened and uninterested in anything, let alone focused on reading. At this moment, after getting out of bed, she was sitting at her desk by the window, staring blankly at the two tall willow trees next door. Xiao Ju stood at the doorway, repeatedly knocking. Menglan turned her head and saw her holding a cloth bundle, hands raised above her head, smiling, "Miss, try on the new clothes that have arrived." Menglan stood up, took the bundle, feeling it was quite thick and heavy. She said, "Wasn't I only having a lined jacket made of green satin? Why is there so much?" Xiao Ju smiled, "The clothes inside are beautiful." Menglan, feeling somewhat puzzled, placed the bundle on the bed, opened it, and the first thing that caught her eye was a bright red color. It was a lined jacket of light red silk, trimmed with large red satin. Without looking at the folded clothes below, she knew there was a light red silk skirt. She frowned at Xiao Ju and said, "Who told you to bring this? Are these my clothes?" Seeing her slightly widened eyes and rosy cheeks, Xiao Ju put a finger in her mouth, took a few steps back, and lowered her head, unable to lift it. Menglan pointed to the bundle, "This is heavy. You brought it, you have to take it away. If you don't, I'll hit you." Seeing the situation was bad, Xiao Ju turned and ran downstairs. Menglan didn't dare look at the bundle on the bed, picked up a book, placed it on the table, and looked at it intentionally or unintentionally. But she heard leisurely footsteps approaching from behind. She guessed it was Xiao Ju again; this child liked to meddle, and the more you paid attention to her, the more she would cause trouble. She fixed her eyes on the book, ignoring everything else. At this moment, a hand quietly rested on her shoulder. She shrugged, saying, "I'm not in a good mood, don't bother me." As she turned her head, she saw her mother standing by the chair with a slight smile. Menglan immediately stood up and said, "Mother, you've come to my room too." Madam Jiang smiled, "You're being childish again. I asked Xiao Ju to bring the bundle upstairs. If you want to blame someone, blame me." Menglan said, "I...you're not...I don't like..."

A Poem on Twenty-Four Gentlemen

— (Sun Shouchang)

On this year's Lantern Festival, Mayor Wu invited He Wuliang, Gu Bangjun, Qian Xinzhi, Zhang Xingyan, Wang Boyuan, Jiang Yiping, Wu Xingya, Li Dachao, Chen Jicheng, Chu Minyi, Zhu Wenqi, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Pan Gongzhan, Xi Yushu, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, Mei Lanfang, Chen Guangfu, Xu Xiaochu, Gu Shaochuan, Sun Daosheng, Xu Jiji, Lu Shoulian, Chen Xiaodie, and others to a spring banquet at the International Hotel, where the Datong Music Society played "White Snow in the Sunny Spring," a grand occasion of the time. Yesterday, I received a seven-character ancient verse from Chen Xiaodie from Japan, asking me to compose a matching poem, incorporating the names of the above gentlemen, which is not easy to do. I transcribe it below:

The round moon shines on He "Wuliang" in the fifteenth,

Where gentlemen like "Bangjun" gather for a spring cleanse.

Cups float on the winding stream of "Xinzhi",

"Xingyan" sets the rules upon the banquet.

The wine god "Boyuan" is full of vigor,

Absorbing all the spring red as smooth as a whetstone.

"Yiping" enjoys a carefree life in this time,

Awakening "Xingya" from a dream, the European wind blows.

The heaven and earth are as expansive as "Dachao's" eight diagrams,

Stars are scattered, resembling "Jicheng's" assembled heroes.

"Minyi" should not be haggard,

Temporarily finding solace in the lonely tung tree.

Spring wind tailors the embroidered gauze for "Wenqi",

Rippling "Yuesheng's" delicate flower shadows.

Suddenly rising from the ground with a majestic appearance,

A fierce tiger "Xiaolin" emerges from its lair.

The red clouds are dense, and "Tiesheng" is not open,

A righteous man willingly dies for his country.

Ape Duke reads the green jade book,

Sitting and "Yansong" contemplating the clear moon.

Ten thousand apertures blow, and "Xiaolai's" sounds increase,

"Lanfang's" carriage returns with exceptional aura.

Xi He strikes the sun, and "Guangfu" emerges,

The overflowing peach blossoms form a "Xiaochu" knot.

The cloud and water are vast, the road five thousand,

The red forest leaves bear "Shaochuan's" white aura.

Knowing that the ancient "Daosheng" is now,

The ten-day week passes in "Jiji's" every moment.

Who can ascend with "Shoulian" to heaven and earth,

And jointly drink and listen to "Sunny Spring's" "White Snow"?

Night on Avenue Edward VII

— Dawn

The night on Avenue Edward VII is built upon the city's erotic culture.

Under the neon lights, the large clock of the "Red Seal Tobacco Company" has not yet passed 12. Here, there are thousands upon thousands of people bustling about. Around the Great World amusement center, the shadows of nightingales and the sounds of music linger, spreading with the flowing air.

On the stretch of road from East Xinjiao Bridge to the Great World, women stroll or walk. On their rough skin, they apply white lead powder. Most of them are those who sell their bodies. Under the social structure of erotic culture, the middle class and proletariat alike are idols of flesh.

Like the lingering nightingales, prostitutes, Shangbai girls, glass girls, and Russian wives, they struggle under the whip of life, similarly creating many deformed people under erotic culture. When night falls, these skeletons dance on this long Avenue Edward VII, as the neon lights redden half the sky.

At the intersection of Rue Zhu Bao San, many neon lights of "BARs" or "CAFEs" flicker. In the hazy night, there are foreign sailors wearing white sailor hats and baggy pants, or French sailors wearing red caps, all wanderers on the Huangpu River or in the colonies. They sway like drunken men, humming vagabond songs.

Fat arms and fat thighs of White Russian aristocratic women, slender figures, and oily black hair of Chinese misses, exuding strong musk in the white powder, scatter throughout this night on Avenue Edward VII. Listening to the jazz music, facing this array of fragrances, they shake the hearts of many wanderers!

The night on Avenue Edward VII is built upon the city's erotic culture.

The Beautiful Night on Avenue Joffre

— Yafei

The beautiful night on Avenue Joffre is like a beautiful prose poem, like a French salon painting, even more like a mysterious dream. Here, I believe that if there were a romantic poet, or a sensual essayist, or even a symbolist artist living here, then there would definitely be a great successful work for us to appreciate.

The autumn night on Avenue Joffre has the tranquility of a virgin, the tenderness of a young woman, the abandon of a prostitute, and the sentimentality of a wanderer. Especially just after dusk, strolling with a few friends, looking at a row of distant, flickering streetlights, seemingly a long string of pearls. If one were to look from one end of Avenue Joffre to the other, the dazzling strip of light in the middle would have such a seductive meaning. It would even make one suspect that they were in Paris and forget that they were still in their homeland!

Avenue Joffre is full of French flavor. We only need to see the neatness of the streets, the style of the shops, and the displays in the windows to rarely find any Chinese flavor.

Among the many roads in Shanghai, Avenue Joffre, like North Sichuan Road, has a mysterious color. This road, full of exotic atmosphere, is as straight as a riding whip, from Ba Xianqiao to Avenue des Soeurs, this long stretch of road is as wide and flat as a still river, perfectly straight without a single curve. French plane trees are planted on both sides of the sidewalk, arranged like troops waiting to be inspected, a solemn and orderly air that makes people excited.

Many bizarre and romantic stories often occur in those Russian restaurants and taverns. Every time it is late at night and quiet, when general shops and companies are closed, the Russian restaurants and taverns are just beginning to be lively.

The French Concession is a place of refuge for most White Russians. The men wander the streets all year round, while the women, in addition to selling their bodies to make a living, also work as maids to get by. Although they also have a motherland, their motherland has forgotten them. Although they also have a home, they can no longer return to their own homes. They can only flee to foreign lands, spending a miserable and wandering life forever. Therefore, in this lonely midnight, they can only bring a cavity of hidden resentment, a cavity of depression and boredom, make an appointment with a few companions, and go to the Russian restaurants or taverns to drink inferior beer, get drunk, and stumble out. Some sit alone in a dark corner, silently drinking coffee, recalling the glorious history of the Tsarist era, their past glory, and their current decline. The memory of this story gives him eternal sorrow. They hate the Bolsheviks, but all of this has become a past dream, and now hating and now reminiscing are also in vain.

They also joke with the waitresses, and sometimes when they are drunk, they think of the past situation and cry bitterly. This romantic tragedy is the expression of their inner sadness.

In some cafes, in this quiet night, a melodious, Pizhena voice gently flows out, flowing out, drifting in the streets, drifting on the leaves of the French plane trees. In the charming singing of the young girls, some optimistic European men and women leisurely sit, drinking sweet wine and singing love songs.

Avenue Joffre sometimes gives people many stimuli, but sometimes it also gives people much comfort!
