The Shanghai News Medical Journal

On the Pessimistic Views of Our Medical Community Regarding the National Elections

— Wang Qizhang

Since the promulgation of the National Assembly Representative Election Law, the people of the whole country have focused on various points in the election law that are related to their own positions. Among them, some cannot understand it, some suspect injustice, and some feel obstructed. The affairs of the general office are many, and the brains of the Law Interpretation Committee are particularly taxed. But in the final analysis, things are never fair in this world. It is common sense to cry out when there is injustice. Therefore, there is a lot of noise and many arguments. Our medical community is, of course, unable to escape this door of right and wrong. So recently, there are those who wave flags and shout, those who draw swords and cross bows, those who slam the table and roar, and those who sigh. But whether they are active or passive, they are still nothing more than men of passion and husbands who care about national affairs. Compared with those who are silent and indifferent, they are better in the end. I can now write down several reasons for the pessimistic views of people and publish them to the country and offer them to my colleagues. Let everyone see the benevolent and the wise, and each follow their own conscience.

(Theory A) The fundamental reason why freelancers are not included in citizens but are specially singled out is that they have a kind of specialized knowledge that is outstanding. The country especially respects their profession and highly regards their personality, which has the meaning of looking at them with different eyes. For example, like lawyers, accountants, engineers, doctors, pharmacists, journalists, educational groups, university teachers, and those who are self-taught, there are a few. Those who call themselves schools and colleges have not been recognized by the Ministry of Education of the government, nor have they been included in the education system by the government. And this kind of background figures are exactly the same as the masons and carpenters of the engineer class, the account-keeping old gentlemen of the accountant class, the court scribes and malicious officials of the lawyer class, the morning paper sellers of the journalist class, the pharmacy workers of the pharmacist class, and the rural school teachers of the educational group university professors. Saying that they can be included in the same category as qualified, knowledgeable, and scientifically knowledgeable doctors and let them compete in the election can really be said to be their bad luck. It is better to be clean than to lower one's own personality and collude with them to make trouble. Therefore, they advocate giving up the right to vote and not voting.

(Theory B) Traditional Chinese medicine does not have a legitimate organization because we already have a medical association in various places. It has been established for many years. According to the organization law of the same industry association, there must not be a second trade association of the same nature within the same region. Therefore, we believe that the National Medicine Association organized by traditional Chinese medicine is an illegitimate organization. That is, the second trade association of the same nature within the same region. Then how can they have the right to recommend? Suppose that the local competent authority recognizes their organization and allows them to register. We can say that it must be recognized that their organization is not the same nature as our medical association. That is the easiest to understand the facts. But why are they inserted into our medical and pharmaceutical associations in this election? According to this method of messing around, we only have one way to give up the right to vote.

(Theory C) Regardless of what our Premier Sun once said, science can save the country. Even if we forget this testament, we should also understand the world situation and advocate attacking from the scientific side to find a way out. But now there is a group of people in the country who insist on raising the metaphysical traditional Chinese medicine to eight feet high. Even in this election, some people are playing tricks in it, wanting to monopolize it with one hand. In terms of traditional Chinese medicine, they do not care about the qualifications, only relying on the fact that there are many people who think that a show of hands can make our science humiliated. Bah, whether or not to represent, there is nothing rare. This kind of behavior is despicable, dirty, and unscrupulous. It is really hateful. We now urgently hope that the people in charge will express a true attitude, and do not need to be ambiguous and afraid of both sides. Suppose it is to promote scientific medicine and to enrich the country and strengthen it. Then the metaphysical medicine that is out of date should be abolished. Otherwise, there is no need to open any foreign-style medical schools or build any foreign-style hospitals. The foreign-style medicine in the army and on the market is even more unnecessary. But this election must take care of both sides. Under the disparity in the number of Chinese and Western medicine, give us a puppet-style mixed election. Call us to enter the muddy water vat together and promote its corruption. If everyone votes, we will always be disappointed more and successful less. It is better to reveal the inside story and automatically give up the right to vote. It is still fragrant and crisp.

(Theory D) It is said that a so-called Central National Medical Center has been active for a month and has issued instructions to contact the National Medical Associations in various places to prepare for the election. Recently, we have also seen the so-called Central National Medical Center's instructions in the Medical Association and the National Medical Association. When I first saw it, I was stunned. I thought I was seeing things. Later, after a closer look, I started to laugh. It turns out that the Central National Medical Center can not only give instructions to their National Medical Association, but also give instructions to our Medical Association and the National Medical Association. What a presumption. Aren't we all clear? The first article of the National Medical Center rules clearly states that it is an academic institution. And its organizational law uses the method of electing directors. It is by no means an administrative official appointed by the government. Can academic institutions use instructions? I have not studied the rules of this official document style. Or it is the latest regulations, and it is not known. However, we are ignorant and have seen it for the first time. The director is proficient in law and is currently the President of the Supreme Court. I think it will not be a mistake, it will not disturb the regulations, it will not create a precedent, and it will never give instructions to our police association and the National Medical Association, which are irrelevant. And this strange phenomenon, I am afraid, is always a group of ignorant gentlemen sitting in the well. Once they hold the chicken feathers, they treat them as arrows and act recklessly in their inquiries. This generation has more than enough to do evil, but not enough to do good. We mix with him in one breath, and in the end there will be no good results. It is better to be elevated. Therefore, it is advocated that the mixed election will not be changed. I never want to vote.

In short, voting or not voting is a personal freedom. I think it is not a problem. However, according to the above-mentioned numbers, it seems that they are all pessimistic because of indignation. But pessimism is by no means a good method. And the few votes of the new medical community are missing. In the facts of the election, it will never have any impact. But I always think that the government wants citizens to elect and wants professional groups to elect. His purpose is to finally want him to vote. Do not give up the obligations of citizens and their own rights. Moreover, the government naturally treats the people equally, without likes and dislikes. In case of indignation and passivity, although there is no obstacle in the election, there will still be a stain in the history of the election. So I hope everyone is calm and consider it again. It seems more appropriate.

A Record of the St. Blasien Lung Sanatorium (Part 1)

— Ding Huikang

St. Blasien, S. Blasien, is a German translation of the Pearl of the Black Forest in Southern Germany, a holy place for sanatoriums. In recent centuries, scholars have emerged on the relationship between tuberculosis treatment and climate, which has been well known to the world. However, in fact, the climate of general high mountains is not completely suitable for the treatment of tuberculosis, especially pulmonary tuberculosis. However, the medium-sized mountains of St. Blasien have mostly good effects on various types of pulmonary tuberculosis. This kind of not very huge but average stimulus has an extremely beneficial effect on the ability to strengthen life and the tendency to improve the healing of the disease. The extremely small amount of scattered temperature in the mountains has the function of saving the vitality of the disease and promoting the healing of tuberculosis, which is something that the high mountain climate cannot reach. The danger of excessive stimulation, for fresh pulmonary tuberculosis, or excessively weak and neurotic patients, which cannot be tolerated in the high mountain climate, can be avoided here.

Above the Albra River, a tributary of the Rhine River, there is a valley, 800 meters high, which is the famous Black Forest of Southern Germany. The St. Blasien Valley is located between them. From north to south, the peaks are aligned, like a natural barrier. The sanatorium faces south to north, almost surrounded by pine ridges, with exceptionally rich sunlight and sky light. The ground air pressure is low, the air does not contain woven seats, the wind direction is stable and there is little fog, it is cool in the late summer, and there is more sunshine in the winter. In addition, the transportation is convenient and the construction is fierce. After a lot of scholarly climate research and proof, it has become a suitable climate for tuberculosis sanatoriums.

History The St. Blasien Sanatorium began to treat pulmonary tuberculosis as early as 1882. The founder was Dr. Paul Haufe. Since then, it has gradually expanded. In 1895, Dr. Albert Sander added a new building, expanding from 35 beds to 120 beds. From then on, the reputation of the sanatorium has increased day by day, and it has attracted the attention of doctors and patients from all over the world.

In 1914, Professor Bacmister took over as the director of the hospital. Bai also served as a professor at the University of Friborg and devoted himself to effective treatments, such as light therapy and surgery.

The sanatorium is located among the green meadows of the pine ridges, with a peak of 1,200 meters high, facing south. In the space of 150 meters, new gardens were built between 1923 and 25. The hills were decorated with bean sheds and flower racks, and there were fountains, with splashing beads and flying jade, and the flowers were like brocade. Even in late autumn, it presents a magnificent look. It is pleasing to the eye for patients to recuperate here. If you lie down and rest, a wooden shed is built for it, which can be used in both summer and winter.

The internal arrangement is aimed at being beautiful and hygienic, and it does not lose the style of the home everywhere, and there is no stimulation of the hospital scene. All corridors, stairs, lounges, large restaurants, and isolated small dining rooms are designed by experts. For example, the huge windows of the lounge are filled with evergreen plants, giving people a special kind of comfort. The four walls of the large restaurant are made of marble, in brown and yellow, so that there is no cold feeling. The four murals are symbols of the soil, water, and fire, painted by Professor Heerte, and their meaning implicitly implies that the four are the source of health.

All the equipment in the hospital meets the conditions of hygiene and is easy to clean. The floors of all corridors, toilets, stairs, and public places are cleaned with oil. The material is silent Linoleum. Disinfection is performed after the patient is discharged from the hospital. The heating equipment in the hospital adopts the low-pressure steam method. All bedrooms have hot and cold water masks, all made of marble. The wardrobes are all located inside. Each room has a telephone, which can be used throughout Germany. The south of the room is a veranda for lying down and resting, equipped with radio equipment. If there is anything that requires a doctor or nurse, each room has a bell and light device to find it in the shortest time.

Outside the office downstairs, there are consultation rooms, operating rooms, ENT consultation rooms, X-ray rooms, chemical test rooms, dental offices, etc. Male and female bathrooms are separated. There is also a hot water treatment room, which can perform various steam and sitz baths and foot baths. Washing is done by steam. There is a barber shop and a grocery store in the hospital, as if it is a world apart.

Treatment Generally, patients with serious illnesses and no hope of recovery are not accepted. If there are progressive chronic lung diseases, pleurisy, tracheal asthma, chronic bronchitis, gland diseases, and "preventive treatment", such as patients with hereditary diseases, or patients with acquired weakness, they can get the result of improving resistance here. In short, the climate of St. Blasien is most suitable for the treatment of various lung diseases. It is worth noting that for patients with fresh early-stage pulmonary tuberculosis, according to recent expert research, it is not suitable for high-altitude sanatoriums. It is in this mountain climate with a very slight difference in temperature (that is, without severe stimulation) that the best treatment conditions have been found.

Sanitary Common Sense for Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Diseases

— Tang Renjin

(96) Morphological Abnormalities of the Nasal Septum

Anatomically, the nasal cavity can be divided into the nasal vestibule, the proper nasal cavity, and the accessory paranasal sinuses. The proper nasal cavity has one opening in both the front and the back. The anterior opening, which connects to the outside, is the anterior naris. The posterior opening, which connects to the pharynx, is the posterior naris. The nasal septum divides it into the left and right cavities. The position of the nasal septum is almost vertical. It is shaped like a plate and the left and right sides are usually symmetrical. It is formed from a bony and cartilaginous base. The bony part is called the bony nasal septum. The upper part is the perpendicular plate of the ethmoid bone. The back part is the vomer. The cartilaginous nasal septum is the quadrangular septal cartilage that fills the anterior defect of the bony nasal septum. There are two main types of morphological abnormalities of the nasal septum: one is due to the thickening of the covering mucosa (which is caused by chronic rhinitis), and the other is due to abnormalities of the bony or cartilaginous base. According to the abnormality of the base of the nasal septum, we can divide it into hypertrophy and curvature. The hypertrophic shapes can be further divided into two types: spurs and crests. The shape of a spur is sharper. The shape of a crest is longer. Clinically, there are two main causes of nasal septum morphological abnormalities:

(1) Trauma - such as fractures or dislocations of the nasal septum. Children often fall easily, causing external forces to act on the nose, resulting in nasal septum deformities. In adulthood, it is also often caused by trauma, but it is often accompanied by abnormalities in the external shape of the nose.

(2) Developmental abnormalities - one is excessive development of the nasal septum.

The other is a narrowing of the upper and lower diameter of the nasal cavity on the palatine bone. The nasal septum is comparatively oversized. This situation is most common when breathing through the mouth due to adenoid hyperplasia.

The main symptom of this condition is unilateral nasal obstruction on the curved or hypertrophied side, or unilateral reflex neurological symptoms (such as migraine headaches and unilateral tinnitus, etc.). However, compensatory hypertrophy of the turbinate mucosa on the opposite side sometimes occurs, often causing bilateral nasal obstruction. If we use nasal speculum for examination, we will know that the site of occurrence of nasal septum deviation is often in the midline. There are many types, and the scope is also different. Commonly there are C-shaped curvature, S-shaped curvature, C-shaped curvature with crests, and curvature with sharp spurs, etc. (refer to the attached diagrams). The curved side not only protrudes, but the other end is also correspondingly sunken. Compensatory hypertrophy of the turbinate is commonly seen on the sunken side of the curvature. If it is a spur or crest, the other side is mostly flat. Sometimes it can touch the turbinate on the same side. At this time, the resulting reflex neurological symptoms are often severe.

The treatment of nasal septum deviation, spurs, or crests can only be sought through surgical operation. Surgical correction or removal is possible. Among the surgical methods, the one we appreciate the most is the Killian septoplasty. There are about four conditions suitable for performing the operation: (1) when there is a high degree of nasal obstruction, (2) when reflex neurological symptoms are significant, (3) when intranasal procedures are obstructed (such as washing for suppurative diseases of the paranasal sinuses and Eustachian tube ventilation, etc.), and (4) as a preparatory operation for other types of intranasal surgery.

Diagram of Various Types of Nasal Septum Deviation

A—C-shaped Curvature

B—S-shaped Curvature

C—C-shaped Curvature with Crests

D—C-shaped Curvature with Crests on Both Sides

E—Curvature with Sharp Spurs

F—Biconvex Septum

G—Hypertrophic Nasal Septum with Crests on Both Sides

Native Medicinal Plants (Continued)

— Zhou Mengbai

Labiatae

1. Common Selfheal (Brunelia vulgaris, L.)

(Plant) It grows naturally in the mountains and fields and is a perennial herb. The stem is square, usually creeping on the ground, about 0.3 meters high, and the whole plant is densely covered with fine hairs. The leaves are opposite, with long petioles, oval or lanceolate, with entire or dentate margins, and rounded ends. The terminal spike-like inflorescences bloom with purple labiate flowers in early summer, rarely white ones. After flowering, the flower spikes turn dark brown, looking like they are dead, hence the name "Xiakucao" (summer withering herb).

(Crude Drug) Xiakucao (Chuzhou Xiakucao) Herba Brunellae, is the dried flower spike collected. Market products are mixed with stems and leaves. Only those that are purely flower spikes are considered good products.

(Ingredients) The whole plant contains 3.5% of soluble inorganic salts, of which about 68% is potassium chloride. It also contains a substance resembling an insoluble alkaloid.

(Pharmacology) Decoction of Xiakucao, filtered by membrane analysis, yields total inorganic salts, which, when injected intravenously into rabbits, immediately causes a decrease in blood pressure and an increase in respiratory movement, and also exhibits a significant diuretic effect. Experiments with other potassium salts also show the same effect. Therefore, the main physiological effect of Xiakucao should be attributed to its potassium salt content. The alkaloid in this plant has no significant physiological effect.

(Medicinal Use) It is traditionally said that Xiakucao has a diuretic effect and is used to treat gonorrhea. It has also been used as an important medicine for scrofula since ancient times. — Daily dose 5-10 grams, in decoction.

Example prescription: Erwei Xiakucao Tang, used to treat scrofula.

Xiakucao 8.0 grams, licorice 1.0 gram

Decoct above into 200 ml. Take in three divided doses daily. Depending on the condition, Ligusticum chuanxiong, rhubarb, and forsythia can be added.

Q&A on Dental Common Sense (43)

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 228) If a tooth is extracted and not replaced, what effect will it have on the adjacent and opposing teeth?

Answer: Because there is no resistance, adjacent teeth will gradually become sparse, and opposing teeth will gradually grow out.

(Question 229) If one tooth is missing, how many teeth should be installed in the replacement?

Answer: There are usually two types of inlays. The first type requires only one porcelain tooth with a rubber or metal plate underneath, riding on the gums. This is called a denture. The second type requires three gold teeth (except for front teeth), one solid in the middle and two hollow on the sides, fitted over the adjacent teeth on the left and right, just like building a bridge. This is called a bridge. If two adjacent teeth are missing, the denture should have two teeth, and the bridge should have four teeth, and so on.

(Question 230) It is said that the old-fashioned tooth extraction in China involved a "bone-separating powder" that caused teeth to fall out painlessly on their own. Is this true?

Answer: I have also heard this said many times and have tried to find this medicine, but have not been able to. If this medicine is truly valuable, able to make teeth fall out on their own without anesthesia or pliers, then someone should have promoted this miraculous Chinese medicine and developed it on a large scale, and we should be able to see hospitals using "bone-separating powder" for tooth extraction everywhere in Shanghai! Why is it buried in the countryside, hiding like a hermit, letting Master Ma and Brother Pliers solve all tooth extraction problems? It can be seen that this medicine is unreliable.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Crackdown on Extra Tips in the Hotel Industry

— Fang

The Municipal Hotel Industry Association, in order to discuss the issue of extra tips, convened a temporary membership meeting at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. The meeting resolved that it was impossible to accept the provisions in the implementation method that stipulated that no security deposits could be taken and that tips given by guests should be turned over as aviation donations. Generally speaking, if there are already tips, why should there be extra tips? This kind of extra tip should be cracked down on.

However, in reality, the extra tip is often not given to the general waiters and porters, but is mostly distributed to the accountants and managers. This is a practice in the Shanghai hotel industry that has become almost legal due to custom. Since this kind of tip is distributed to the accountants and managers, the waiters and porters have to solicit tips from customers separately, hence tips have become extra. In essence, it is adding a tip on top of a tip, which is fundamentally unreasonable.

Furthermore, this kind of tip is often not voluntary from the customer, but is mostly extorted. For example, the regular tip is stipulated as one, while the extra tip must be two, three, or four. For example, the other day a friend went to a hotel and rented a room for $1.20, stayed only one night, and the next day gave an extra tip of 20 cents. The porter refused to accept it, saying that rooms here have never taken a tip of 20 cents. As a result, he paid 40 cents, and looking at his face, he was still not completely satisfied. This kind of illegal extortion from guests is deeply hateful.

Renting a room already includes a tip, and then there is another tip on top of that. This not only shows no consideration for customers, but also makes excessive demands, which inevitably makes people afraid to go forward. This custom has become a trend, and it is quite difficult to reform. However, examining the reasons why this trend has developed, half is due to the various demands of the porters, and half is also due to the cultivation by some customers. Shanghai was originally a pit for spending money, and the hotel industry has become half a place for entertainment, regarding money and legal tender as if it doesn't matter at all. This lavish behavior is caused by about three types of people:

1. Wealthy young masters, spending money like dirt, giving generous tips to show off their wealth. 2. Those who have nothing to do after work, playing mahjong in eight rounds, winning or losing a lot, not counting the tips, so-called gambling money is the easiest to find. 3. Socializing openly, equality between men and women, compatible language, eyes inviting hearts, then the hotel industry is also an excellent place for dating. This kind of behavior naturally doesn't count the tips, and is even more generous. With these three types of people, the appetites of the porters have been cultivated, so in addition to giving a regular tip, they also give an extra tip to them. Not only will they be rejected outright, but they will also be regarded as "rural bumpkins". Therefore, those who don't want to be bumpkins have no choice but to generously empty their pockets to win the porter's favor.

However, this kind of extra tip is naturally happily paid by the above three types of people, but ordinary honest businessmen and poor travelers are naturally very unwilling to pay this kind of tip that should not be paid. Therefore, the government's order to crack down on extra tips in the hotel industry is extremely necessary and shows a lot of consideration for guests. However, there are many obstacles to implementation. If you want to crack down on extra tips in the hotel industry, you must first fundamentally correct the regulations of the hotel industry.

It is said that the hotel's porters are not only required by the hotel to pay a security deposit, but also not paid wages. Therefore, those who work as porters rely entirely on extra tips for their livelihood. If they are cracked down on, then the porters' livelihoods will be exhausted. As for the security deposit, it is even more difficult to cancel, because most of the people who work as porters are idle people, and not many have sound character. If they see the customer's money and valuables and get ideas, although the hotel has regulations that money and valuables should be handed over to the accounting room, the procedures are too cumbersome and difficult to withdraw, so it cannot be fully implemented. Therefore, if you want to crack down on extra tips and cancel security deposits, you must first fundamentally transform the organization of the hotel industry.

Lakeside Words

— Lv Gang

Last night I could hardly sleep all night. I don't know what kind of psychology it was, but I always felt a bit ethereal in my heart: it seemed like a dewdrop was mixing on a lotus leaf, or like a piece of duckweed was floating on the water... I couldn't make it calm down no matter what. I can't say why, and I don't want to put the momentary actions of instability into those "malicious" words "not in their right mind" like you did. I know your original intention was naturally not like that. Because in fact it wasn't a question of whose "mind was confused." For a person, a thing, a kind of will, and the cause to which we are loyal... we have not been negligent. We have paid a lot of enthusiasm in our work. We are not stingy at all. This is not for anything else, and it can't be said that it is something that a person in a state of confusion can consciously do. This just illustrates the serious attitude and enthusiasm of a person with a career mind.

Of course, I don't blame you for having doubts about this matter, as long as it doesn't hinder your understanding of real life. I think it's not too much for a young person to have a skeptical attitude when understanding life. We often yearn for a future life, and we are often amazed by some new things, just like when you first started on this road, you felt a little uneasy and apprehensive. In fact, when you take each step steadfastly and firmly, you will just feel that this is just: "So that's how it is!" This is because we are still like children and don't quite understand human relationships and social customs. We can't put on a straight face to live our lives! We use the heat of youth to open up this difficult road. As you said, we can't live in a muddle-headed way, but a monotonous life makes us quietly lose our enthusiasm for our careers. I very much agree with what you said about promoting our work through mutual encouragement. I think that only in the same career of will can we quietly reduce the doubts and hesitations about this kind of thing.

I usually often warned you. In the attitude of trusting a person and looking at a thing, you should observe from both positive and negative sides. You also said that you often make this careless mistake. I really didn't expect you to inadvertently start from this place that doesn't need to be doubted. This result will inevitably lead you down the opposite road. In human understanding, this is a cruel tragedy—and it is also from here that the tendency of idealism arises. I hope you are not as bad as described here and can quickly restrain yourself. Just like your criticism of me.

I respect you very much, especially your enthusiasm for your career. This morning, in a clear and gentle climate, I did not expect you to give me such sincere advice. If the train wasn't about to leave, I really couldn't bear to leave you with a painful smile. Things also happened to coincide. As soon as I got on the carriage, the train immediately started. If I was only one minute late, I would have missed the train. It was really lucky that I didn't miss it this time.

After the train started, my heartstrings were much calmer, and I didn't feel tired at all. I was actually able to finish reading two books on the train, which was unexpected. I reread "This is Just Spring". Some drizzle floated in through the window, startling me, and I then noticed the green wilderness in the suburbs, the blue mountains, the blue sky connecting with the green mountains... The car slowly crawled through the fields, passing one town after another, gradually approaching Songjiang. The time it stopped in Songjiang was not long, but it suddenly evoked an image in my mind. I imagined those sixty-odd young companions who came back from Songjiang. They were the same as us. Lost... I was angry, but I couldn't say a word. I silently looked at the small station, the platform, and the endless fields: I thought of the vast mountains and forests of the three eastern provinces mentioned in "A Corner of the Metropolis"...

At noon, the train finally stopped in Hangzhou.

We wandered around the lakeside for a while. The weather here wasn't as hot as most people think it is. Maybe it was because it was cloudy, and a cool breeze was blowing across the lake... It actually rained heavily in the afternoon, which was really unlucky, and our plan to tour the lake today had to be temporarily suspended. I didn't sleep well last night, so I took the opportunity to take a satisfying afternoon nap.

The night slowly unfolded, and we took a walk by the lake. Because we were worried that it would rain again at night, we didn't dare to be "night tourists". Bu and I were talking about the past years ago, which was really a bit unbearable to look back on!...

I hope tomorrow will be a sunny day, so that I can rest well at night. Seeing the distant fire by the lakeside, I thought of the meaning of the words "light" and also of the spark of fire pressing on my heart. I am willing to send you a hidden fantasy.

San Taro (Continued)

— Lin Na

Seven or eight brothers were already lined up on the small open space outside the door. He gave them a brief and dry explanation, then issued an order to take the team towards the river. At the end of the river, in that gloomy, pitch-black darkness, they would find a small, damp house, which was now guarded by two armed soldiers. They had to open the door and drag out each of those criminals, lining them up in a vast wilderness; then set up machine guns, pull the firing pins and shoot sparks at them, taking them to another ethereal world.

Suddenly, his nerves spasmed sensitively, and his eyes were unnaturally filled with many shadows, angry faces, and tragic cries. In these shadows, in these faces, in these cries, there were the most familiar and the most unfamiliar to him: yet, they were all equally powerfully moving him, causing him pain. Slowly he remembered again, remembered his mother, who had been widowed when he was young and was now a female worker in a yarn factory, remembered her wrinkled, thin face, remembered her low voice.

"I can't keep you, people won't allow me to keep you, but you must remember clearly: I want the gift you bring me back to be the cries of foreign brothers, not the glory of the Emperor..."

He sighed bitterly and whispered to himself, "There is no hatred, we originally had no hatred!"

...His footsteps gradually slowed down unnaturally, and finally stopped. His eyes stared blankly into the distance, at the shadows of people wriggling slightly, at the damp little house immersed in darkness. Then, he slowly reached out, tore off the military cap that flashed the golden light of the cap badge, threw it hard on the ground, and turned his head and walked away in dismay.

When I was in Dalian

— Shi Dai

The second time I went to Dalian was during the first anniversary of the establishment of Manchukuo. The military police and detectives (i.e., detectives) in Dalian were busy without rest, and the docks, train stations, and hotels were full of security nets everywhere. Before I left Yantai, I had already written a letter to a fellow villager who worked at the Beef Company to smooth out our relationship so as to avoid accidents in the future. The fellow villager sent a quick reply, and everything was done according to my wishes, so I boldly went to Dalian. On the ship and at the dock, I went through several interrogations by detectives. I answered fluently, and they even called my fellow villager's company to verify my identity. They acknowledged that I was indeed a member of their company, so there were no problems. However, they were still somewhat suspicious of me. They kept paying attention to my demeanor and clothes, as if they had already determined that I didn't look like a Beef Company employee. However, they couldn't find any flaws.

With the enthusiastic hospitality of my fellow villager Mr. Yi San, I settled down in their company. But the detectives were miserable. They came to this place every day, especially the cross-eyed one nicknamed "Mole" (Dalian people call locals "local bumpkins"). He came every day, sitting outside the counter, drinking tea, smoking cigarettes, and the clerks were all laughing and joking with him, because in Dalian, merchants dared not easily offend these people - detectives! Although he tried every means to get my secret from here, he took great pains, and he couldn't make a business deal out of me!

At first, Mr. Yi San accompanied me everywhere to visit fellow villagers and friends. Later, he said not to go out to look for people anymore, as this would easily arouse suspicion from the detectives and military police. If you just go to brothels, watch plays, and gamble at clubs every day, then you can be safe. These entertainments, except for watching plays, which I was slightly interested in, gambling and prostitution gave me a headache! So Mr. Yi San led me to stroll through the night market, stroll through the gardens, and sometimes go to opium dens to play around. Because he didn't have that much time on weekdays, we could only go to Xigang on Sundays to listen to Liu Kuitong's Shanghai-style opera. Sure enough, it worked well, and the detectives never came again.

"Why not try everything in the world, learn about it, come with me?"

Another fellow villager said to me like this. I felt that his words were right, and I should learn about everything. So I followed him to clubs, opium dens every day... Sure enough, I learned about many things I had never seen before. Those terrible things, countless Chinese people are buried in that terrible devil's den. I simply shuddered! I dare not go to see those shocking things again! That tyrannical master who used dangerous conspiracies to kill innocent slaves! How vicious! How cruel! It used the iron hand of power to cover the sun, let the light retreat behind the darkness, and recklessly slaughtered the slaves!

One night I went to the Naniwa-cho night market and met Gao Yunfeng at the door of "Liaodong Department Store". He was a chef in "Iwakura Yoko," and when he saw me, he insisted on taking me to his house to sit down. Naturally, I couldn't refuse, so I followed him to his house. To my surprise! He already had a family now, a young wife, and two boys who could already run! What surprised me the most was that his wife was actually a ×× girl. So I immediately had a bad impression of Yunfeng in my mind, "Why marry a ×× woman, maybe he will be loyal to ×× forever?"

We were talking, but she was standing aside without saying a word, her face full of melancholy and sadness, and her skin was a bit yellow, probably because she had quarreled with Yunfeng. But I couldn't help but ask Yunfeng:

"Why doesn't your wife speak? I hope to talk to her."

Yunfeng didn't say a word first but sighed! He looked at his wife, then lowered his head and said to me in a low voice:

"Linzi's (referring to his wife) brother, Ueki Saburo, originally worked at the South Manchurian Electric Company. In the spring, he was arrested and imprisoned for suspicion of inciting a strike, but was eventually released due to insufficient evidence. Later, he joined "Dalian Kisen Kaisha" as an accountant. During the Battle of Gubeikou, he and three young people secretly wrote wartime slogans everywhere. Unexpectedly, he was arrested again. This time he suffered severe torture, and his left arm was broken! His father heard the news about his son and immediately went to the government to declare that the country should severely punish this kind of traitor! He no longer recognized him as his son. As a result, Ueki Saburo was sentenced to death! He and his three comrades were shot the day before yesterday. Linzi had the best relationship with her brother. Now that her brother is dead, how can she not be sad? Even I am very sad. I lost a good friend!"

Seeing Yunfeng and his wife both shed tears, I was silent for a long time without saying a word.

After dinner, I returned to Shuanghe Sheng Beef Company. The clerks were putting up the door panels. As soon as I entered the door, the third boss asked me: "Mr. Qin, where did you go? Yi San was worried and went outside to look for you!"

When Yi San came back, I said many words of apology to him. In bed, I thought of Ueki Saburo.

"We lost a friend!"

Under the Sunlight

— Shu Mang

That intensely hot weather is here again. During the day, the sun bakes the asphalt streets of the metropolis, even melting the asphalt. People rush about under the sun, planning for the day’s living, their minds dizzy, their eyes a little blurred, walking unsteadily, as if about to collapse.

"If I could really just fall down and not have to worry about anything, not have to worry about any more hard times, that would be great." Old Guan couldn't help but think miserably like that as he walked in the scorching sun. The monkey performing tricks squatted on his shoulder, baking like a stove, and the little spotted dog he held by a leash with a bell hanging from it had its tongue stretched out long, presenting a terrifying sight. The heavy burden of miscellaneous goods pressed heavily on his other shoulder, cumbersome like an endless ancestral ritual of cruel reality. Also, his skinny, monkey-like fourteen-year-old child and twelve-year-old adopted daughter shouldered the practice spears and broadswords, struggling to follow behind the middle-aged man in his forties (but who looked more than ten years older than he was), tirelessly running around in the scorching summer sun, exhausted and worn out...

"Another hot day has arrived," As soon as he thought of this, Old Guan felt a sour feeling rushing up in his heart. The helplessness and cruelty of life made him feel a little uncomfortable - wasn't it also a hot day when he fled from his hometown with his wife and children, desperately seeking refuge? The wandering bandits in the fields were terrifying: they had also gone hungry for ten days in a row, had been dragged off to jail, and had begged without success... Over the past year, his wife had died under the grind of life, leaving behind two skin-and-bones children, squeezed into a group of vagrants, taught to use spears and batons, taught obscene ditties and Lianhua Luo ballads, while the father in his forties, with his graying hair, had been forged even crueler by the cruel life. He broke his children's bones, as if administering a poisonous punishment, while he waited with a terrifying grin for the audience to toss down one or two copper coins... (To be continued)

Storytelling with Stringed Instruments

Cao Xiaoying's Yu Qing Ting

Central-Western (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening Verse: "Floral Moon Linked Pearls"

The Spring River Flower Moon Night is most flourishing. The moon reflects the flower wall, flowers and moon together. Flowers love the bright moon, flowers love the moon. The moon moves the flower shadows, the moon moves the flowers. Flowers bloom waiting for the moon, the qin stops sounding. In the moon, urging the flowers, the drums beat wildly. The ground is covered with fallen flowers, golden ten-thousand characters. A crescent moon, a jade hairpin. The flowery world is always in spring. The monthly tide is always on time. The bright moon polishes a jade axe. Plum blossoms play on a bronze pipa three times. Jiang Lang's dream revolves around a flowering pen. Zhang Ziyou floats on a moon raft like an immortal. The face is like a peach blossom, the eyebrows like the moon. The moon in the water, the flower in the mirror. It's good to rely on the moon elder to convey the mandarin duck love story. Ask the flower slave to pick up the phoenix hairpin. Worshipping the moon and burning incense, emotions are sincere. Burying flowers and pitying jade, resentment is endless. Reed flowers, autumn moon, Xunyang guest. Lonely moon, plum blossoms, hermit's home. The moon palace broadcasts good news, startling the sweeping star. Flower steps with moon, phoenix-headed shoes. Opening Verse: "Daiyu Burning Drafts"

Wind and rain for consecutive nights, iron horses noisy. Good flower branches deserted in the Grand View Garden. There is no sound in the Xiaoxiang Pavilion. There is a, sick beauty with tears hanging. Heart anxiously. Tears hanging. Sound silently. Night long. Listen to that, the sound of gongs and drums over the wall. Meeting the maid, Qin Fang Gate. Zhou Zhenyu's Righteous Demon Transmission

Yuan Chang (1120) 12:45 AM to 1:30 AM

Opening Verse: "Curtain Letter" (Mimi Collection Inaugural Issue)

It is lamentable, Han Xin of the past. He was originally, a struggling, wandering person in the Jianghu. At that time, he had not met the true lord of the Han Emperor. He seemed like, a dragon losing water, suffering. One day, he encountered an old woman washing cotton wadding. Begging for a meal, feeling deep gratitude. Later, repaying kindness with thousands of gold. He had no money, wandering the streets. Carrying a Longquan sword on his back. He was unwilling, to be teased by the butcher's children. He disregarded, the shame of suffering humiliation under the crotch. He abandoned his pen to join the army and enter the Han army. How could he, with a well-thought-out plan, not encounter good fortune. All because of, bragging after getting drunk. Almost, bound to the city to be executed and crippled. Therefore, he secretly ran away in the dark. Unexpectedly, Xiao He chased Han Xin in the moonlight. Fortunately, Xiao He was in Han.
